rin chen gter gyi mdzod chen por ji ltar bzhugs pa'i dkar chag dang /
smin grol rgyab rten dang bcas pa'i brgyud yig dngos grub sgo brgya 'byed pa'i lde'u mig ces bya ba bzhugs so //

oM swasti bi dza yan+tu /
byin rlabs sprin las dngos grub bdud rtsi'i char //
phab pas grub gnyis snye ma mchog sbyin pa'i //
rtsa gsum 'dus zhal bla ma mtsho skyes rjes //
phan bde'i dpal yon rtag tu 'jo bar mdzod //
dgongs pa brda dang snyan khung shog ser tshig
/bka' babs lung bstan brgyud pa nor bu'i phreng //
'dod rgu yid bzhin stsol mdzad de kun kyang //
dad gsum gtsug gi rgyan du bsten par bgyi //
rim dgu'i theg pa'i dkyil 'khor rab 'byams dang /
khyad par bsam yas lhun stug bkod pa'i rgyan //
nang rgyud sde gsum zhi chags 'bar ba'i lha //
mi 'bral snying dbus dwangs ma'i thig ler bzhugs //
bde chen ye shes skyed mdzad mkha' 'gro'i tshogs //
thugs brtser dgongs te gnang ba'i skabs dbye zhing //
rgyud gsum dam can rgya mtshos gsang ba mchog
/'dzin skyong spel la phrin las g.yel med sgrubs //
rgyal bstan spyi dang khyad par snga 'gyur lugs //
skye dgu kun dang lhag par gsang sngags kyi //
gdul byar gyur la phan 'dod lhag bsam ni //
g.yo zol med pas tshul 'di bsgrub la zhugs //
gangs can ljongs 'dir sras bcas rgyal rnams las //
thugs rje phul byung sangs rgyas gnyis pa des //
dus la dgongs te thugs brtses gdams pa rnams //
srog ltar gces pas tshig re'ang ngal brgyas btsal //
gal chung chos kyi phyogs su ma byas shing //
lhag par phyogs ris chos spong snying khams med //
chos la chog shes bral bas tshe gcig tu //
gsang chen zab mo'i smin grol don du gnyer //
rgyal ba'i thugs rje dus las mi yol phyir //
mos pa'i ri mgor nyi 'od lhung ba las //
rgyun yod nges pa'i gter rnying phal mo che //
legs par thos shing lugs srol ma 'dres shes //
shin tu dkon pa 'ga' yang bde blag rnyed //
dka' bas btsal rnams don yod bya ba'i phyir //
gces dgu phyogs gcig bzhugs na dpe lung rgyun //
phan par 'gyur snyam 'dod blo thog mar skyes //
'on kyang tshod yod gzu lum ma byas par //
bka' babs bdun ldan yongs rdzogs bstan 'gro'i mgon //
pad+ma 'od gsal mdo sngags gling pa dang //
rtsod bral gter ston mchog gyur gling pa ste //
gu ru dngos dang mtshungs pa'i gter chen gnyis //
dpang du bkod nas don 'di rung mi rung //
rung na gnang ba zhu bar gsol btab pas //
dag pa'i snang bar gu ru'i gnang ba thob //
nye brgyud byin rlabs snga rjes mang du gsan //
sdud 'os go rim rkang grangs dkar chag bstsal //
ngo mtshar gter rnying mang po rim par brdol //
phal cher bka' babs lung gis dbugs kyang phyungs //
des na byed mang phal dang mi mnyam pas //
pad+ma'i rjes su zhugs kun mdzod chen 'di //
dad pas spyod par mdzod dang rmad byung dbyig
/ci 'dod 'jo bas 'phral yun 'tshengs par 'gyur //
gang gi tshe phyogs bcu dus bzhi'i bde bar gshegs pa thams cad kyi khyab bdag gdod ma'i mgon po dpal kun tu bzang po nyid sku gsung thugs lhun grub stug po bkod pa'i rgyan dam par bzhugs te /
sa bcu'i rgyun mtha' la nye bar son pa'i 'phags pa mchog rnams nas bzung /

gnas rigs drug gi yid can rgya mtsho'i rdul snyed kyi bar mtha' yas pa'i gdul bya'i don 'bad rtsol mi mnga' bar ngang gis rdzogs par mdzad pa las re zhig gsung rdo rje nA da'i dbyangs kyis sgra brnyan dang mthun par       theg pa sna tshogs pa'i chos phung 'dod dgur 'jo ba'i tshad ni sems byung dang bcas pa'i blo can su zhig gis bzung bar nus /
de lta mod kyi bsdu ba la rnam par dga' ba rnams kyi ngor /
spyi mdo dgongs pa 'dus pa'i rgyud las /
kun 'byung 'dren dang dka' thub rig
/dbang sgyur thabs kyi theg pa 'o //
zhes rnam pa gsum dang /
de las nang gses kyi dbye bas theg pa'i rim pa dgur bzhag pa las /
gtso bor gsang sngags snga 'gyur ba'i grub pa'i skyes bu rnams las rim par 'ongs pa'i dbang sgyur thabs kyi theg pa nang rgyud sde gsum gyi rdo rje'i gnas zab cing rgya che ba'i snying po las kyang snying por dril ba'i gzhung dang man ngag rab 'byams      shig gangs can ljongs su 'khod pa'i skye dgu'i bsod nams kyi mgron du byon pa la ring brgyud bka' ma zhes grags shing /
rma gnyags gnubs gsum la rim par bka' babs shing so zur gyi mkhas grub chen po slob brgyud dang bcas pa rnams kyis bstan pa yun ring bskyangs /
'on kyang snyigs ma'i shugs bdo bas bstan pa'i rgyun srol nyag shin tu phra bar gyur pa na /
lo chen bai ro tsa na nyid bsam bzhin bstan 'gro'i dpal du byon pa chos rgyal gter bdag gling pa dang /
g.yu sgra snying po'i rnam 'phrul gcung lo tsA ba d+harma shrI sku mched /
sna nam bdud 'joms rdo rje'i yang srid rdor brag rig 'dzin chen po pad+ma phrin las rnams kyis bstan pa'i me ro bslangs par mdzad cing /
smin gling phyag rjes rnying ma bka' ma'i legs bshad pusta ka bkra shis rtags kyi grangs ldan snga 'gyur bstan pa'i snang byed mkhas grub gzhan phan mtha' yas kyis ru dam o rgyan bsam gtan chos gling du spar la bkod pa dang /
dbang lung sgrub mchod kyi rgyun srol snga 'gyur gyi chos sde chen po rnams su dar zhing rgyas par bzhugs bzhin par snang la /
'dir bka' bsdu'i rtsol ba cung zad bya ba ni nye brgyud gter mar grags pa'i chos rnams te /
de la don lnga /
gang bsdu bar bya ba'i chos /
ji ltar sdud pa'i tshul /
de ltar bsdus pa'i dgos pa /
grub don bzhugs tshogs dngos 'chad pa /
smin grol nyams len bya tshul sogs gal che'i gnad kyi gdams pa brjod pas mjug sdud pa'o //
dang po ni /
dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas ma lus pa'i gsang gsum phrin las dang bcas pa gcig tu bsdus pa'i rnam thar 'chang zhing khyad par gangs can bod kyi skyabs gnas gcig pur gyur pa o rgyan gyi slob dpon   chen po pad+mA ka ras bod yul skal ldan rje 'bangs rnams la gsang sngags rdo rje theg pa'i zab chos dngos grub rnam pa gnyis gang la ji ltar dgos pa sgrub pa'i thabs    so so'i khams dbang skal pa'i rjes 'gro bsam las 'das pa bstsal /
gsang ba'i bdag mo ye shes mtsho rgyal gyis bka' bsdu mdzad /
rje 'bangs lo tsA so so la smon lam gyi bka' gnyer gtad /
ma 'ongs snyigs ma'i mthar thug pa'i bstan 'gro skyob byed kyi btsas su brtse bas dgongs te gter rigs bco brgyad kyis mtshon par zab mo'i rgyas btab /
rnam 'dren lnga pa'i bstan pa ma shar gyi bar du gang la gang 'dul gyi dus dang 'tshams par 'byung bar byin gyis brlabs /
dus la babs pa'i tshe sngon gyi las 'phro dang smon lam sad pa'i gter ston sprul pa'i skyes mchog rnams kyis rim par spyan drangs nas 'gro don mdzad pa rnams te /
de'ang kha byang yod pa'i ming can bye ba /
kha byang med pa'i ming med bsam las 'das pa sbas par gsungs pa dang /
bod yul sa 'og thams cad gter gyis bkang //
ri brag thams cad sgrub gnas byin gyis brlabs //
zhes dang /
nga yis bod khams gter gyis bkang nas yod //
dngos grub 'dod na gter gnas kun nas longs //
zhes gsungs pa'i don mngon du gyur nas gter chos sngar byon dang gsar brdol shin tu mang bas thams cad sdud par mi nus shing /
phyogs zhen tsam gyis blang dor dbye bsal chos spong gi las ni bgyi ba ga la spobs /
'on kyang gter ston grub thob thams cad kyi rgyal po mchog gi sprul sku gsum /
'khrul med gling pa bcu gcig gtso bor gyur pa sngon byon bstan 'dzin mkhas grub chen po rnams la yongs su grags pa'i gter rnying rigs la gzhi byas /
phyis byon chos dang gang zag tshad mar gyur kyang dus skabs rten 'brel dbang gis kha gcig gi snyan lam du mtshan tsam yang 'byon du mi btub pa mang du snang ba rnams ni re zhig btang snyoms su bzhag
/yongs la grags shing nga khyod kyi phyogs 'dzin chung ba'i phyis kyi gter chos phal mo che rnams kyang dkyus su bkod pa'o /
!
/gnyis pa ji ltar sdud pa'i tshul ni /
spyir snga 'gyur bstan pa'i rgyan gcig 'og min o rgyan smin grol gling gtso bor gyur pa'i khungs dang ldan cing sel med kyi brgyud pa rnam par dag pa'i yongs 'dzin rnams las zab gter du ma'i smin grol phyag len 'bad rtsol chen pos zhus shing /
gtso che ba rnams kyi bsnyen sgrub re'ang bgyis /
khyad par slob dpon chen po 'jam dpal bshes gnyen dang chos rgyal khri lde snyigs dus bstan 'gro'i mgon du bsam bzhin srid pa'i rol gar bsgyur pa /
bka' babs chen po bdun gyi mnga' bdag thams cad mkhyen pa 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po'i zhal snga nas gter rnying 'ga' zhig gi smin grol bka' drin tu thob pa na /
gter phran sngon byon phal cher dbang lung lta zhog dpe rgyun tsam yang 'byor dka' bas de dag phyogs bsdu zhig gi rtsol 'dod blo thog mar skyes /
de tsam gyis kyang dngos grub rnam gnyis sgrub pa'i thabs yongs su mi rdzogs pas mgo rkang tshang ba zhig byung na rang gzhan la phan par re ba'i blo gnyis pa skyes te 'char gzhi'i tho yig bcas /
kun mkhyen bla ma rin po che'i snyan dbang du zhus shing gsol ba btab pas shin tu dgyes pa chen pos thog mar legs so'i dbugs dbyung dang ji ltar bsgrig bya'i go rim sa bcad zhib mo bstsal /
bar du sngar ma thob pa phal mo che'i smin grol dang /
lhag par gter rnying dpe lung gi rgyun sngar nas chad pa mang po yang gter du byon pas mtshon nye brgyud kyi byin rlabs du ma dang bcas te rjes su gnang mthar gzhan phan phrin las kyi sgo 'phar dbye bar mdzad pa sogs bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i bka' drin bstsal pa la brten pusti kha shas grub pa'i skabs su /
sprul pa'i gter chen mchog gyur gling pa'ang yid ches rtsod bral gyi phrin las dbu tshugs pa'i thog mar rung min brtag pa gnang bas rung nges pa'i lung byang dmigs bsal thob /
bar du tshogs kyi 'khor lo bcas gnang ba lan gsum zhus par gter ston brgya rtsa spyi dang bye brag dmigs su bsal ba kha shas kyi gter chos nye brgyud du gsan 'dug pa rnams kyi smin grol gdams gtad zhus /
mthar rje nyid kyi gter byon mdo dang sgyu 'phrul gtsor gyur sngar sa steng du ma byon pa rnams kyang skal pa bzang po'i dpyid du nos pa de dag la brten nas 'di nyid sdud pa'i rtsol ba la zhugs pa yin gyi /
thos pa tsam la snying por bzung nas ma brtags pa'i gya tshoms dang /
gsang ba gnyan po la ji mi snyam pa'i ras chod /
'gran sems dang grags 'dod sogs log pa'i sems bskyed sngon du btang bas ni ma yin no /
!
/gsum pa de ltar bsdus pa'i dgos pa ni /
bdag lta bu shin tu ma sbyangs la mi mkhas shing ma bsdams pa'i so skye bya bral nyam chung bstan pa'i khur mi theg pa zhig gis skabs su ma babs pa'i bya ba rlabs chen brtsam pa 'os su ma gyur kyang /
byis pa'i dus nas rgyal dbang pad+ma 'byung gnas la mi phyed pa'i dad pa brtan po lhan skyes su mnga' bas de'i gsung gsang ris su ma chad pa la 'dun rtsol chog shes med pa shugs 'byung du grub pa dang /
bod spyi'i mtshan nyid gsar nges kyi dbang du song bas gter rnying phal cher zhi bar mnal la nye zhing rgyun dkon pa 'ga' yang chad du phangs pa dang /
gter rnying gsar du byon pa rnams ni mtshan tsam las chen po rnams kyi gsan lam du'ang 'byon ma btubs pas snying ltar gces pa dang /
gter gsar phal mo che'ang rang gzhan la nye bar mkho ba shas che zhing dkor sdud kyi phyag cha dang /
lto phyir bon gyer mkhan rnams kyis kyang rjes gnang dang mdos gtad sogs zhu thob dkon pas dkyus gcig tu bkod na de tsam la'ang phan par re ba dang /
tshad ma'i gter chos phyogs re ba'i phrin las can du gyur pa dag kyang gu ru rin po che'i rjes 'jug yongs kyi spyi nor du gyur na ci ma rung snyam pa sogs sgo du ma nas lhag pa'i bsam pa kho na yid la byas te bka' yi bsdu ba la nye bar zhugs pa'ang sangs rgyas kyi byin rlabs         'ba' zhig tu rig par bya ste /
yon tan rin chen sdud pa las /
rgyal ba'i nyan thos pa dag gang zhig chos ston dang //
'chad dang rig pa dag dang ldan par brjod pa dang //
mchog 'phags bde ba byed dang de yi 'bras thob pa //
de dag kun kyang de bzhin gshegs pa'i skyes bu'i mthu //
zhes gsungs pa'i phyir ro /
!
/bzhi pa bka' bsdu la brtson pa'i grub don smin grol gdams ngag gi bzhugs tshogs dngos dang zhar byung brgyud rim gyi tho yig bcas dgod pa la gsum /
gang las byung ba brgyud pa'i lo rgyus /
byung khungs de ldan gyi gdams pa'i dkar chag
/de las byung ba'i gdams skor dngos kyi rnam grangs so //
dang po ni /
gdams ngag khungs dang 'brel ba zhes mkhas pa rnams la gtam du grags pa'i phyir thog mar yid ches pa'i 'byung khungs lo rgyus thos pas de'i gdams ngag la dad cing nges shes 'drong ba'i dgos pa thog mar 'byung bar      'brel la /
de'ang gdams zab 'di rnams kyi ston pa ni sangs rgyas kun 'dus gu ru rin po che pad+mA ka ra ste de'i rnam par thar pa ni sangs rgyas kho na'i spyod yul las gzhan gyis tshad bzung bar ga la nus kyang /
gu ru nyid kyis rjes su gnang nas bka'i sdud pa po rnams kyis bkod pa la /
ji skad du /
rnam thar stong phrag bcu dang brgya phrag dgu
/ma 'ongs dam ldan don du bkod nas sbas //
zhes grangs tshad yod pa dang /
ming can ming med kyi gter kha bsam las 'das par gu ru'i rnam thar sna re bzhugs pas grangs tshad med pa'ang bshad pa las /
gter byon phal mo cher rdzus skyes kho na'i rnam thar du rigs mthun cing bka' ma phur pa'i lo rgyus dang ba mkhal smug po'i gter ma sogs kha cig tu mngal skyes su'ang bshad pas /
yongs grags lugs srol gnyis su bzhugs pa'i /
dang po la rgyas bsdus 'dra min mtha' yas pa zhig snang ba las /
'dir gter byon bka' thang thams cad kyi rtsa ba'i phyi mo nyang ral nyi ma 'od zer gyis dpal gyi bsam yas khams gsum zangs khang gling nas spyan drangs pa /
slob dpon chen po pad+ma 'byung gnas kyi skyes rabs chos 'byung nor bu'i phreng ba zhes bya ba le'u zhe gcig can rnam thar zangs gling mar grags pa /
de'i don bsdus gsol 'debs nyang rin po ches mdzad pa /
o rgyan mdzad pa bcu gcig gi gsol 'debs rat+na gling pas mdzad pa rnams bzhugs /
lung brgyud ni /
o rgyan rin po che /
sdud pa po ye shes mtsho rgyal /
mnga' bdag khri srong lde'u btsan /
gter chen nyang ral /
la stod pa mi bskyod rdo rje /
mdo bo ras pa /
dbus pa grags 'bum /
mnga' ris dpal seng /
bsam 'grub rgyal mtshan /
dkon cog mgon po /
mnga' ris paN chen /
nyang kun dga' lhun grub /
karma gu ru /
mnga' bdag sprul sku
/chos dbang kun bzang /
rig 'dzin phrin las lhun grub /
chos rgyal gter bdag gling pa /
rgyal sras rin chen rnam rgyal /
'gyur med skal bzang 'phel rgyas /
rig 'dzin tshe dbang nor bu /
kun mkhyen chos kyi 'byung gnas /
rgyal dbang bdud 'dul rdo rje /
dpa' bo gtsug lag chos rgyal /
'dren mchog dge legs rgya mtsho /
des bdag blo gros mtha' yas la'o //
yang na rin rnam nas khri brgyud bar ma chad par /
sangs rgyas kun dga'/
'gyur med yid bzhin dbang rgyal /
pad+ma 'od zer /
mkhan dkon mchog 'od zer /
de las so //
gsol 'debs snga ma ni /
nyang yab sras /
gnyos zhig
gnyos sgom rdo rje /
gnyos ston grags pa /
grags pa bkra shis /
mthing ma grags 'od /
grags pa rgyal mtshan /
tshul khrims 'byung gnas /
shes rab rgyal po /
nam mkha'i mtshan can /
mkha' klong yangs pa /
skal ldan rgya mtsho /
rgya ma mi 'gyur ba /
'bri gung rin chen phun tshogs /
chos rgyal phun tshogs /
bsod nams rin chen /
phrin las lhun grub /
gter bdag gling pa /
sras rin chen rnam rgyal nas rim par brgyud de /
pad+ma gsang sngags bstan 'dzin /
'gyur med bstan 'phel /
de las so //
phyi ma ni rat+na'i tshe sgrub gsang 'dus sogs dpal yul phyogs nas brgyud pa dang 'dra'o //
gnyis pa 'phags yul thun mong ba la yongs su grags pa'i tshad thub kyi legs bshad rje btsun thams cad mkhyen pa tA ra nA thas mdzad pa'i slob dpon pad+ma'i rnam thar rgya gar lugs yid ches gsum ldan tsam bkod /
lung brgyud ni /
rje btsun rin po che /
rgyal tshab rin chen rgya mtsho /
blo gros rnam rgyal /
ngag dbang phrin las /
kun bzang dbang po /
gtsug lag dga' ba /
tshe dbang kun khyab /
karma rat+na /
karma 'od gsal 'gyur med /
de las so //
de dag gi 'phros las brtsams te /
o rgyan rin po che'i rnam thar bka' thang don bsdus gsol 'debs rje bla mas mdzad pa ngo mtshar u dum+ba ra'i phreng mdzes /
lung rje nyid kyis bstsal pa'o /
gter ston grub thob rim par byon pa rnams kyi rnam thar mdor bsdus bkod pa rin chen baiDUr+Ya'i phreng ba /
de'i don bsdus gsol 'debs rgyas pa /
mtshan sdom gsol 'debs bsdus pa bcas bzhugs /
'di nas brtsam mdzad byang ma smos pa thams cad rang nyid kyis gsar bsgrigs byas pa sha stag lags so /

/gnyis pa byung khungs de ldan gyi gdams pa'i dkar chag dngos ni /
dkar chag zhib mor bkod pa 'di nyid de bka' rgya'i skor rnams ni zur du gsal la /
zhar byung gang las brgyud pa'i rim pa'ang tshol bde ba'i phyir phyogs su bkod mod /
phrin las dar rgyas su gyur pa kha cig ni brgyud srol tha dad pa'i rnam grangs mang du 'dug kyang 'dir yig tshogs la 'jigs nas rtsa ba sna re tsam las ma bkod pa 'dod na gzhan du rtogs par bya dgos pa dang /
gter phran 'ga' zhig dang gdams ngag phran tshegs 'ga' re sngon gyi dpyod ldan chen po rnams kyi gsan yig tu'ang bar skabs kyi brgyud pa mi gsal ba dang 'ol tshod du bkod pa'ang yod rigs su 'dug cing /
rang gis zhu yul kha shas nas kyang rgyun yod nges pa'i bla ma dag las gsan nges pa tsam las brgyud rim ma rnyed pa mang rung /
rang nas ni re re bzhin du zhus nges pa las lung tsam yang ma mnos pa'i yig cha sna gang rnyed bsdus pa ni gcig kyang med la /
khyad par snga 'gyur rnying ma'i phyogs su dag snang dang nye brgyud la tshad mar mdzad pas de ltar na /
nye brgyud kyi bka' dmigs bsal du babs pa'i rtsod bral gu ru'i rgyal tshab gter chen rnam pa gnyis las kho bos spyi dang bye brag gi smin grol byin rlabs bka' gtad rjes su gnang ba bcas yang nas yang du yid tshims par zhus shing thob pa lags pas go sa mtho zhing grags 'byor ldan pa zhig yin na bka' babs lung bstan gyi brgyud par ngoms kyang ngoms rin chog pa yod do //
'di'i 'phros las /
smin grol 'bogs pa'i lag len dang bcas gshom ji ltar bya ba'i tho yig kyang nyer mkho'i ched du bkod pa'o /
!
/gsum pa de las byung ba'i gdams skor dngos dang /
tha mar dge ba'i slad du gsang sngags lam rim zhal gdams smon shis dang bcas pa'i skor gnyis so //
dang po ni /
'od gsal rdzogs pa chen po'i rgyud rdo rje sems dpa' snying gi me long las /
bskyed pa ma hA yo ga ni chos thams cad kyi gzhi lta bu'o //
rdzogs pa a nu yo ga ni chos thams cad kyi lam lta bu'o //
rdzogs pa chen po a ti yo ga ni chos thams cad kyi 'bras bu lta bu'o //
zhes bskyed rdzogs sde gsum du gsungs pa las /
dang po bskyed pa ma hA yo ga'i skor la gnyis /
rgya che ba rtsa bar gyur rgyud sde dang /
zab pa lag len du 'dril ba sgrub sde'o //
dang po la'ang spyir sku gsung thugs yon tan phrin las lnga'i rtsa bar gyur pa'i rgyud sde lnga /
sgrub pa lag len du ston pa rol pa'i rgyud sde lnga /
spyod pa yan lag tu 'gro ba'i rgyud sde lnga /
ma tshang ba kha skong ba'i rgyud sde gnyis /
de thams cad kyi khyab byed gzhi'am rtsa ba lta bu gyur pa spyi rgyud rdo rje sems dpa' sgyu 'phrul drwa ba dpal gsang ba'i snying po ste tan+t+ra chen po sde bco brgyad du grags pa las /
dpal rdo rje sems dpa' sgyu 'phrul drwa ba zhi khro so so'i dbang /
rgyud kyi bshad pa /
sku'i rgyud sangs rgyas mnyam sbyor rigs bsdus pa'i dbang /
spyod pa yan lag tu 'gro ba'i rgyud sde'i nang gses glang po che rab tu 'bogs pa'i dum bu dri ma med pa bshags pa'i rgyal po'i rgyud kyi rjes su 'brang ba zhi khro khrom bkrugs dang /
cha mthun yi ge brgya pa dbang mchog rgyal po'i rgyud sogs la brten pa'i zhi khro rigs bsdus kyi dbang /

kyi lung sogs rgya cher bzhugs pa ni bka' ma'i skabs su song ba yin la gter ma'i phyogs la rgyud lung bka' ma dngos mtshungs sngar ma byon kyang deng skabs mchog gling zab gter las byon pa sogs 'god du yod pa dang /

/snyan brgyud zhag bdun ma'i gsal byed lcags zam bdun pas mdzad pa /
gur sgrom dpe'u ris /
rim lnga'i khrid pad phrin gsung bcas nyer mkho'i yi ge tshang ba bzhugs /
spyir bla sgrub skor lnga yongs su rdzogs pa glegs bam gnyis tsam gyi lung rgyun yang bzhugs shing /
khra tshang pa blo mchog rig pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa'i dbang bsgrig dang las byang /
pad phrin gyis mdzad pa'i bsnyen yig dang lam zab gsal byed sogs lugs srol 'di la gal che nges pa'i legs bshad tshad ldan rnams bzhugs mod /
'dir khyer bde nyung ngu gtsor bton nas bkod pa ste 'og ma rnams la'ang shes par bya'o //
de la dbang gi brgyud pa ni /
chos sku snang ba mtha' yas /
longs sku thugs rje chen po /
sprul sku pad+ma 'byung gnas /
mkha' 'gro ye shes mtsho rgyal /
gu ru chos gyi dbang phyug
/sman lung pa mi bskyod rdo rje /
dwags ston dbang phyug rdo rje /
gnyan ston ye shes rdo rje /
se sdings sangs rgyas dpal /
de sras yon tan bzang po /
gu ru chos sku 'od zer /
mtshungs med dpal 'byor dbang phyug
/sprul sku chos kyi dbang po /
rig 'dzin karma gu ru /
rgyal sras karma dbang 'byor /
blo mchog rig pa'i rdo rje /
rig 'dzin pad+ma phrin las /
grub dbang pad+ma dbang drag
rdo rje tshe dbang nor bu /
kun mkhyen chos kyi 'byung gnas /
bka' brgyud phrin las rnam rgyal //
rdo rje 'chang pad+ma nyin byed dbang po /
des bdag la'o //
yang na /
karma gu ru nas /
grub chen kun bzang dpal 'byor /
rig 'dzin phrin las lhun grub /
o rgyan gter bdag gling pa /
rgyal sras rin chen rnam rgyal /
khri chen pad+ma bstan 'dzin /
'gyur med phrin las rnam rgyal /
de las rje btsun rin po che 'gyur med phrin las chos sgron dang /
mchog sprul pad+ma dbang rgyal gnyis /
gnyis ka las khri chen 'gyur med sangs rgyas kun dga'/
kun gzigs 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse /
des bdag la'o //
gter gzhung lung brgyud kho bos bla ma dam pa gnyis las lan gnyis mnos pa nang gses brgyud srol mang yang rtsa ba tsam ni khra tshang pa yan dbang brgyud ltar la /
de nas 'jam dbyangs legs bshad rgya mtsho /
'chi med grub pa pad+ma rang shar /
dpang ston gsang bdag rdo rje /
bstan 'dzin ye shes lhun grub /
dpang ston pad+ma tshe dbang /
bstan 'dzin mkhyen rab mthu stobs /
khyab bdag rdo rje gzi brjid /
de las so //
yang /
pad+ma tshe dbang nas /
sgrol ston chos kyi rgyal mtshan /
rje mkhyen brtse ste nyams len byin rlabs zhal gzigs bar ma chad pa'i brgyud pa khyad par 'phags pa'o //
smin lugs ni gter chen /
rin rnam /
o DI ya na /
gsang sngags bstan 'dzin /
dpal 'byor rgya mtsho /
bstan 'dzin chos rgyal /
'gyur med bstan 'dzin 'phel rgyas /
de las so //
snyan brgyud zhag bdun ma'i lung brgyud mdzad pa po bstan 'dzin ye shes lhun grub /
blo bzang bstan 'phel /
bstan 'dzin mkhyen rab mthu stobs /
rje bla ma las so //
bla sgrub 'di dang mtshungs pa rdor gling gsang 'dus ni 'dir byin rlabs chu bo gcig 'dres su bzhugs /
rad gling yang 'dus sogs mtshan mi mtshungs la don gcig pa mang rung 'og tu bla sgrub sde tshan gcig par 'god pa yin la /
yongs dge mi 'gyur rdo rje'i pad+ma badzra grub thob brgya rtsa'i dkyil 'khor dang /
rol rdor brag gter phyag rdor dregs 'dul zhi sgrub bla ma rdo rje 'chang rnams chos sku gtsor bton pa'i zhi sgrub khyad 'phags snang mod /
phrin las kyi gzhung ha cang mang zhing bsham bkod rgyas spros che bas skabs 'dir bsdu ma thub bo //
rgyal sras lha rje'i skye srid gnyis pa rgya lo tsA ba rdo rje bzang po'i zab gter bla ma bstan gnyis skor gsum gyi bcud dril mthong grol 'od kyi snying po rje bla ma rin po cher yang gter du byon pa'i rtsa dbang /
don dbang /
zab khrid /
gter gzhung le'u brgyad pa /
dbang dang las byang gi zin /
spros med sgrub pa'i phrin las dang don dbang gsar bsgrigs bcas /
brgyud pa ni /
chos longs sprul gsum /
chos rgyal yab sras /
mtsho rgyal /
rgya lo tsA ba /
pad+ma 'od gsal mdo sngags gling pa'i zhal snga nas bka' drin du bstsal pa'o //
gnubs chen yang srid dri med kun dga'i zab gter gyi snying po thugs sgrub yid bzhin nor bu rje bla mas brag dmar mgrin bzang nas yang gter du bzhes pa'i smin dbang /
zab khrid /
gter gzhung le'u bdun pa /
byang gter las byung ba'i rgyal chen mchod thabs /
brgyud 'debs /
mchod phreng /
dbang chog gsar bsgrigs bcas /
brgyud pa ni /

mtsho rgyal /

gter ston dri med kun dga'/
pad+ma 'od gsal mdo sngags gling pa /
des thugs rje chen pos dgongs te bka' drin du bstsal pa'o /

/gnyis pa longs sku'i tshul du sgrub pa ni /
bla ma longs sku tshe dpag med rdzong chen tshe dbang /
3)
de'i thems med tshe sgrub bu ston gong khug ma'i dbang /
rdzogs chen la chos sde bdun lhag bzhugs par snang mod 'dir thems med tshe sgrub gter gzhung rtsa ba /
de'i nyams len dang brgyud 'debs zhwa lu ba rin chen blo gsal bstan skyong gis mdzad pa /
bo dong kun mkhyen 'jigs bral chen po'i dag snang tshe dpag med rigs lnga'i dbang chog thugs dam gtor rgyun brgya rtsa las phyungs pa rje des mdzad pa /
de la bu ston gong khug ma rtsa ba'i brgyud pa ni /
gu ru chos dbang /
bla ma tshul khrims bzang po dgung lo brgya dang bcu dgu bzhugs /
chos rje bu ston rin po che /
thugs sras lo tsA ba /
'jam dbyangs grags pa rgyal mtshan /
'khrul zhig tshul khrims rgyal mtshan /
rin chen mchog grub dpal 'bar /

'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug
/dbang phyug rab brtan /
rin chen bsod nams mchog grub /
rin chen bsod nams rgya mtsho /

smon lam bsam gtan /

rin chen blo gsal bstan skyong /
'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po /

de las so //

/tshul khrims bzang po /

paN chen chos kyi rgyal mtshan /

/spyir gter byon tshe sgrub rigs la /
bcom ldan 'das tshe dpag tu med pa gtso bor byas nas sgrub pa dang /
bla ma pad+ma tshe dpag tu med pa gtso bor byas nas sgrub pa'i lugs gnyis su snang ba las /
snga ma ni pad+ma gsung gi zhi sgrub tu 'du zhing /
phyi ma thams cad 'dir 'du ba yin yang phal cher tshe sgrub tsam du sde tshan gcig pa'i dbang du byas nas 'og tu 'byung ba yin no /

4)

las byang gsung rgyun ma /

lo tsA ba rgyal ba mchog dbyangs rnam 'phrul rgya ston pad+ma dbang phyug gis gangs bar phug mo che'i sgo drung pha waM dbang phyug gi mtshan rtags can nas spyan drangs te yang gter du sbas pa'i shog ser gter srung mkha' 'gros spyan drangs nas rje bla ma la phul te gtan la phab pa bla ma bde mchog 'khor lo'i dbang bzhi /

/pad+ma 'od gsal mdo sngags gling pa /
rje des bka' drin chen pos smin grol tshang sprugs su bstsal pa'o //
gsar ma'i dril bu rim lnga'i byin rlabs kyi rgyun deng sang chad pa /
'dir dbang gi skabs su byung zhing khrid kyang don gcig pa la zab gnad mang pos 'phags pa dang /
grub chen dril bu pa'i nye brgyud ngo mtshar ba'ang bzhugs pa bcas zab chos 'di ni kun las kyang khyad par du 'phags pa'o //
bka' 'dus bar pa     spyir bka' 'dus snga phyi bar gsum ste /
snga ma shel brag pad+ma brtsegs pa nas o rgyan gling pas gdan drangs pa'i bka' 'dus chos kyi rgya mtsho /
bar pa bla ma dgongs 'dus /
phyi ma rig 'dzin mnga' ris pa'i gter byon bla ma bka' brgyad rig 'dzin yongs 'dus dang /

dgongs 'dus la'ang sangs rgyas gling pa'i bla ma dgongs 'dus pod bcu gsum /

/gro shul bde chen gling pa snga phyi bar gsum gyi mkha' 'gro dgongs 'dus pod drug ste gsum du grags so //

de'i sgrub pa /
'khor lo'i bri yig

'gyur med bstan 'dzin 'phel rgyas las thob pa ni /
smin gling dang kaHthog brgyud pa gtso che la /

'di la pod chen bcu gsum da lta'i bar du dbang lung nyams len sgrub rgyun bar ma chad cing byin rlabs tshan kha shin tu che ba /
bskyed rdzogs phrin las dang bcas pa ma tshang ba med pa bod yul sa 'og kun gyi gter gcig tu bsngags pa don dang ldan pa'i ngo mtshar can 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po'i gan mdzod lta bu nyid do //
lo chen bai ro tsa na'i sprul pa'i sgyu 'phrul gter chen chos kyi rgyal po rdo rje gling pas ngom shod gnam lcags brag rta mgrin phug nas spyan drangs pa'i zab chos 'dus pa chen po bzhi'i dang po bla ma zhi ba bka' 'dus rin chen gter spungs kyi rtsa dbang chen mo /

bstan 'dzin karma dge legs nyi ma /
des bdag la'o //
lung brgyud nges don rgya mtsho nas /
gter sprul pad+ma bstan 'phel /
bstan 'dzin rin po ches bdag la'o //
che tshang gsung ni mdzad pa po nas /
gar dbang chos rnam la'o //
yang brgyud tshul mang 'dus nyams len byin rlabs kyi rgyun khyad par can gcig ni /
gter ston sku mched /
chos bdag dbang rgyal rdo rje /
grub pa'i rnal 'byor bsam 'phel rtogs ldan gu ru ma Ni /
des so //
'di la chos sde'i rtsa ba gsang ba ye shes snying po'i khrid rgyun khyad par can bzhugs kyang yig tshogs mang bas 'dir ma 'khod do //
rig 'dzin chen po de nyid la snyan brgyud mkha' 'gro'i snying khrag gi skor zhes pa 'ga' zhig bzhugs yod par snang yang spel bar ma mdzad la /
de'i sde tshan mkha' 'gro ye shes mtsho rgyal gyi snyan du brgyud pa gu ru spros med don sgrub kyi dbang /
gzhung rtsa ba /
dbang chog
/dag snang srin yul ma'i dbang /
de'i gzhung gsal byed bcas /
de dag gi brgyud pa bla ma rgyal ba kun 'dus bstan 'dzin rin po che nas brgyud pa de ltar ro //
gnubs nam mkha'i snying po'i thugs sprul kaHthog rig 'dzin chen po tshe dbang nor bu rdo rje gzi brjid kyi dgongs pa'i gter las phyungs pa gsol 'debs bsam pa lhun grub kyi dbang /
dgongs gter rtsa ba'i gzhung /
brgyud 'debs /
dbang sgrub lhan thabs dang dbang bshad dbang chog bcas rje pad+ma nyin byed dbang pos mdzad pa /
khrid kyi zin bris lung zin nye ba'i bu brgyad kyi nang tshan gnyags dz+nyA na'i sprul pa 'ba' ra ba o rgyan ngag dbang ye shes kyis mdzad pa rnams las dbang dang rtsa gzhung gi brgyud pa ni /
chos longs sprul sku
/mtsho rgyal /
nam mkha'i snying po /
'gro 'dul ma Ni badzra /

'ba' ra ba'i khrid yig las khrid lung rgyun /
ngag dbang ye shes /

sman sgom chos rje kun dga' dpal ldan /

gtsug lag chos kyi rgyal po /
karma nges don dpal bzang /
khyab bdag rdo rje gzi brjid /
de las so //
yang na mdzad pa po nas /
kun bzang tshe dbang don grub /
tshe dbang 'jigs med bstan 'dzin /
dpal ldan dpa' bo phyin 'dra /
rig 'dzin chen po'i chos skor rnams rol pa'i rdo rje dang gter kha ma bu'i tshul yin pas 'di'ang bla ma rgyal ba kun 'dus kyi gzhi byed pa phyag len du snang zhing /
dgongs gter dbang dngos khyab brdal du spel bar ma mdzad pa'i ngag rgyun thos so //
mnga' bdag khri lde dang rgyal sras lha rje zung du 'jug pa'i rnam rol bsam yas rdzogs chen pa kun mkhyen 'jigs med gling pa'i dgongs gter klong chen snying gi thig le'i rtsa dbang rgyal thabs spyi blugs /
nang sgrub rig 'dzin 'dus pa'i las byang dang gab byang gter gzhung /

/'gyur med mthu stobs rnam rgyal /

o rgyan gter bdag gling pa dang thugs rgyud gcig pa dge sbyong blo gsal rgya mtsho'i yang srid mthu stobs nus pa'i dbang phyug pad+ma dgyes pa'i snyan brgyud gu ru zhi ba yid bzhin nor bu'i dbang /

yang las byang gi lung /

/yan lag bar chad sel ba rtsa ba'i sgrub skor zla nyin kha la rong sgo'i gter byon phyi ltar bla ma snang srid zil gnon thod phreng rtsal du sgrub pa thugs sgrub bar chad kun sel la rtsa dbang rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum /

khyad par rdor gling dang mkha' 'gro ma kun dga' 'bum pa'i gter chos rnams shin tu gsal bar gnang ba'i rjes su bka' gtad lung bstan dang bcas pa bstsal /

/brgyud pa bka' 'dus zhi khro ltar ro //
rig 'dzin rol pa'i rdo rje'i mtsho gter snyigs dus kyi dam 'gong gdug pa can gyi gnyan por ches zab pa drag po khro rol phur bu la /
sngar lugs brag gter gtor dbang gis bcings pa dang gu ru drag khros dbang la lha sngags kha bsgyur ba sogs kyi rgyun snang yang /

//gnyis pa dngos grub kyi rtsa ba yi dam zhi khro sgrub pa'i skor la /
spyir rigs kyi 'khor los sgyur ba rnam pa lnga las rab tu phye ba'i lhag pa'i lha rab 'byams sgyu 'phrul drwa ba'i sgrub thabs dang man ngag mtha' yas pas tshad gzhal du med kyang /

'di la gnyis /

 bye brag tu sgrub pa'i skor ro /

/lcags 'dra /
yang zlog gi skor /
rdo rje'i rigs 'joms byed 'char kha nag po /
rin po che'i rigs kha thun /
pad+ma'i rigs 'jigs byed ru mtshon dmar po /
las kyi rigs gshor gsang nyi ma khros pa sogs /
khro chu dang /
king kang dmar nag gis mtshon bka' gter gyi gshed skor mtha' yas pa zhig byung zhing /
deng skabs kyang bka' ma gshin rje'i gshed ru mtshon dmar po /
kha thun nag po /
gdong drug nag po gsang rdzogs thugs kyi sgrub pa gsum gyi gzhung yongs su rdzogs pa'i dbang lung /
rgyud sde pod gnyis rab 'byams kyi lung /
gter ma'i gshed skor rang gzhung rkang tshugs dang /
gzhan gyi yan lag tu gyur pa mang po rgyun ma nyams par bzhugs mod /
'dir gal po che kha shas shig 'god pa la gnubs chen yang srid drag sngags thams cad kyi mnga' bdag dum pa rgya zhang khrom rdo rje 'od 'bar gyis gter gnas mang po nas byang chub sgrub pa dang drag po sngags kyi chos sde mtha' yas pa spyan drangs pa rnams kyi gtso bor gyur pa /
'jam dpal tshe bdag nag po'i skor la phung po ri bo che'i gter byon gtso che ba lcags 'dra /
ma'i skor rnams g.yung phu'i rdza lhud mo dang bu'i skor rnams nyug gi rdo rje sgrom bu nas spyan drangs pa'i lcags sdig skor gyi dbang gnyis la /
lcags 'dra pad gnubs kyi lugs gnyis ka'i bka' ma'i dbang gi chu bo'ang gcig tu 'dres shing /
se ston gyi dbang chog lhan thabs dang bcas pa bklags chog tu dril ba'i dbang chog bdud rtsi'i bum bzang rig 'dzin chen po pad+ma phrin las kyis mdzad pa 'di steng nas lcags 'dra bam chen gsang ba'i dbang dang /
lcags sdig mu tig phreng ba'i dbang gnyis chabs cig tu thob pa yin pas de nyid sor bzhag gi spyi dang khyad par gyi dbang bka'/

/sog zlog pa /
gangs ra lo chen /
phrin las lhun grub /
gter chen rje'o //
o rgyan sangs rgyas gling pa'i zab gter zab rgya gsum pa 'jam dpal nag po yang zab thugs kyi tshal pa'i byin rlabs rjes gnang /
rtsa ba bsnyen pa'i las rim /
sgrub thabs las byang dang bcas pa /

byin rlabs rjes gnang /

bye brag grib srung /
de'i yig chung /

/rme ru rtse'i gshor dmar chung /

12)dang /

'dir chags med zhabs kyis gsan yul ma nges pas bar gyi brgyud khungs brtag dgos pa yod cing /
spyir tshe sgrub 'di gter kha gong 'og byang bdag rnams dang mtshungs par mtsho skyes rdo rje rigs 'dus yin 'dug pas bla ma zhi ba'i skabs su 'god par 'os kyang 'dir tshe sgrub tsam du sde tshan gcig pa'i dbang gis bzhag pa'o //
gter chen rdo rje gling pa'i rdzogs chen lta ba klong yangs kyi cha lag zhi khro'i tshe sgrub kyi dbang /
tshe sgrub 'od zer drwa ba dbang chog dang bcas pa /

bcud len te rdo rje phreng ba lnga tshan /
las bzhi'i sbyin sreg
/brgyud 'debs gter gsung tsam las gzhan mi bzhugs shing 'di rnams kyang rgyun phra bas ched du bkod pa'o //
nang sgrub phrin las dbang chog bcas /
brgyud pa ni /
dpal yul nas rim brgyud rdo rje 'dzin pa chen po pad+ma gsang sngags bstan 'dzin las zhus pa ste rtsa gsum 'bras bu'i don khrid sogs dang mtshungs pa phyogs gnyis las byon pa'o //
pad gling tshe khrid rdo rje phreng ba'i dbang gsung rgyun ma /
14)
pad+ma'i rnam 'phrul 'chi med grub pa'i dbang phyug thang stong rgyal pos gu ru rin po che la dngos su gsan pa dang mchims phu'i gter ma zung 'jug tshe rta zung 'brel 'chi med dpal ster gyi dbang /
15)
bsnyen yig
/brgyud pa'i khyad par mang yang 'dir gtso bo 'dod bum ltar dang /
yang na /
grub chen nas /
tre ho chos kyi rgya mtsho /
lo chen 'gyur med bde chen /
mkhas btsun dbang po /
sman khab pa phrin las rgya mtsho /
phrin las lhun grub /
gter bdag gling pa sogs brgyud srol mang du thos /

dbang brgyud ni /
sangs gling thugs chen nang nor bu lugs ltar ro //
bo dong ras chen dpal 'byor bzang po la lhag pa'i lhas dngos su gnang ba'i zab khyad kyi gdams pa ras chen chos gsum du grags pa'i nang tshan /
o rgyan tshe dpag med la dngos su gsan pa tshe dpag med lha bcu bdun ma'i dbang /
tshe sgrub mda' 'phel ma'i chog bsgrigs 'chi med 'byung ba zhwa lu pa rin chen bsod nams mchog grub dang /

zin bris rje bla mas mdzad pa rnams /

tshe dpag med /
'chi med pad+ma 'byung gnas /

chos rje rnam rgyal mgon po /

/gnyis pa zhi ba thugs rje chen po'i smin grol gyi skor la /

rgya mtsho lnga'i gtor dbang /

/gangs ra ba ngag dbang dpal bzang /
A yu tiSh+Tha phyin chad snga ma dang 'dra /

/gnyis pa drag po rta mchog rol pa'i skor la /
sku mdog las mtshon te rigs kyi dbye ba dang bka' ma rgyal po lugs dregs pa lnga dril /
gter rnying gru gu yang dbang gi dregs pa kun sgrol sogs rgya cher byon par snang mod /
deng sang rgyud sde 'ga' zhig gi lung rgyun tsam las bka' ma'i smin grol cher bzhugs par ma mngon /
'dir kaM tshang bka' brgyud la bka' babs pa'i rta mgrin bde gshegs thugs dril gyi las byang rgyal dbang gsum pa rang byung zhabs kyis mdzad pa tsam lung rgyun la bsams nas bkod /

/brgyud pa yang 'dus dpal yul las brgyud pa dang 'dra /
legs ldan bdud 'joms rdo rjes 'bras ljongs lha ri rin chen snying po'i mgul nas spyan drangs pa bdud rtsi 'khyil ba 'chi med tshe'i rgyud kyi dgongs don tshe sgrub bdud rtsi 'khyil ba'i rtsa dbang rgyas pa /

/brgyud pa sman skor spyi ltar la gter chen bla ma rin po ches bdag la'o //
rgyud bdud rtsi bam po brgyad pa dang bka' brgyad bder 'dus gtso bor gyur pa'i bka' gter rgyud lung man ngag rnams kyi zab don 'dus pa'i legs bshad dam rdzas bdud rtsi'i sgrub thabs gsang chen mchog gi myur lam chos rgyal gter bdag gling pas mdzad pa /
sngags byang /
nyer mkho'i zin bris /
bka' brgyad gsang ba yongs rdzogs las sman gyi las tshogs /
lung rgyun dbang dang mtshungs /
sman chig sgrub bya tshul rje bla mas mdzad pa bcas /
!
/gnyis pa bdud rtsi'i skor du phyogs gtogs cha mthun gyi rigs la /

des bdag la'o //
bka' babs phyi ma lha sras mu ne'i rnam 'phrul grub chen nyi zla klong gsal la ring brgyud snga ma gnyis ka 'dus shing /
nye brgyud grub chen dza ha bIr gyis smin grol gdams skor dngos su gnang ba'i zab chos 'ja' lus 'od phung rang grol gyi dbang /
dmar khrid /
gtum mo khrid chen brgyad bcas /
rtsa ba'i yig cha la /
gsol 'debs dngos grub char 'bebs /
bla ma brgyud pa'i rnam thar nor bu'i do shal /
lo rgyus nyi zla zung 'brel /
sngon 'gro byin rlabs thugs rje'i 'od 'bar /

shes rab ma'i nyams len gser gyi yang zhun /
gegs sel bdud rtsi'i char 'bebs /
khyad 'phags khrid chen brgyad dang /
'byung ba'i gegs sel /

'khrul 'khor rtsa 'grel 'ja' lus mchog ster /
dza bIr bla sgrub 'od phung rang grol /

'khrul 'khor bka' rgya ma bde stong 'od phung /

28)gsum gyi dbang /

o rgyan yab yum /

/brgyud pa rig 'dzin 'dus pa dang 'dra /
sprul pa'i gter chen pad+ma 'od gsal mdo sngags gling pa'i dgongs gter zab mo'i chos sde 'chi med 'phags ma'i snying thig las /
rtsa ba'i dbang bskur /
thun mong tshe'i rjes gnang /
yang zab tshe'i byin rlabs /
shangs zab bu lung nas babs pa'i sgrol gzhung rgyas pa'i rtsa ba rdo rje'i tshig rkang /
las byang ye shes snang ba rtsa gzhung /
brgyud 'debs /
sman mchod /
tshogs bsdus /
tshe 'gugs mchog gling gter gzhung /
rgyun khyer nyid mdzad /
rtsa ba'i dbang chog
/byin rlabs rjes gnang gi cho ga
/bdag 'jug
/sbyin sreg bcas /
brgyud pa /
tshe dpag med /

yid bzhin 'khor lo /
shrI sing ha /
bi ma mi tra /
o rgyan chen po /
rje mnga' bdag yab sras /
'bangs lo tsA bzhi /
grogs ye shes mtsho rgyal /
bka' babs bdun gyi mnga' bdag rje btsun 'phags ma dang grub pa'i slob dpon rnams kyis mngon sum rjes su bzung ba pad+ma 'od gsal mdo sngags gling pa /
des bdag la'o //
zhar byung nyer mkhor bzhag pa /
smin gling lo chen gyis mdzad pa'i sgrol ma'i maN+Dal bzhi chog
/lung brgyud mdzad pa po nas /

o DI ya na /

mthu stobs rnam rgyal /
'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse /
des so //
sprul pa'i gter chen o rgyan mchog gyur bde chen gling pa'i gter byon mkha' 'gro'i skor la /
rong me dkar mo stag tshang gter byon dam chos snying po skor lnga las mkha' 'gro dgongs 'dus snying po'i dbang /
gter gzhung tshang ba /
dbang chog
/thugs sgrub bar chad kun sel gyi cha lag ri bo dbang zhu'i brag nas byon pa'i bar chad sel ba'i chos skor bzhi las /
phyi 'jigs pa bcu drug gi bar chad sel ba sgrol ma 'jigs pa kun sel gyi rtsa dbang /
gter gzhung cha tshang /
dbang chog dang maN+Dal gyi cho ga thams cad mkhyen pa 'jam dbyangs bla mas mdzad pa /
de dag gi zur 'debs 'khor gyi lha bskyed /
thugs dam bskul ba'i gsol 'debs sogs /
gter chen de nyid kyi dgongs pa'i gter las phyung pa sgrol ma'i zab tig phyi nang gsang ba'i dbang /
bka' srung bka' gtad gcig brgyud ma /
legs so gsum gyi don khrid /
phyi nang gsang sgrub khrid gzhung bka' srung g.yu sgron ma lo rgyus kyi bar gter gzhung cha tshang /
phyi nang gsang gsum gyi phrin las dbang chog khrigs bkod /
khrid yig
/'bum rdzong gter byon zur bza'i thugs dam skor drug gi mkha' 'gro sgrub pa'i skor gyi phyi nang gsang ba yang gsang gi dbang lnga /
tshe dbang dang bcas pa /
phyi sgrol ma rnal 'byor ma /
nang rdo rje phag mo /
gsang sgrub gsang ba ye shes /
yang gsang man+dA ra ba dang mtsho rgyal sgrub pa'i thabs dang las byang rdzogs rim dbang bskur bcas gter gzhung tshang ba /
spyi 'gro'i dbang bskur gyi cho ga
/ye rgyal nam mkha' mdzod kyi gter byon mkha' 'gro gsang ba ye shes kyi dbang bzhi /
gter gzhung nang gses bcas cha tshang /
phrin las dbang bskur me mchod grib sel sun zlog rnams dkyus gcig tu gsal ba'i chog khrigs bcas /
de dag gi brgyud pa ni /
'od mi 'gyur ba /
gar gyi dbang phyug
/rdo rje rnal 'byor ma /
o rgyan chen po /
ye shes mtsho rgyal /
khri srong lde'u btsan /
dam 'dzin chos kyi blo gros /
'gro 'dul mchog gyur bde chen gling pa /
des bdag la bka' drin du bstsal pa'o //
dgongs gter sgrol ma'i zab tig ni gter chen nyid nas gcig brgyud kyi tshul du /
rje bla ma 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po /
des bdag la 'phags ma dngos mtshungs kyi rten dang lhan cig bka' drin chen por bstsal pa'o //
gzhan yang rdo rje gling pa'i sgrol ma'i rgyud dang man ngag skor zab rgyas /
tshe brtan rgyal mtshan gyi sgrol ma ut+pa la'i skor sogs rnyed na'ang skabs 'dir sbyar ro //
zhar byung gter chen rin po'i gsung /
dbang chog 'khor 'das gzhi grol gyi gcod dbang /
stan thog gcig ma'i khrid /
stan thog gcig ma'i man ngag dang gdams khrid /
dbang chog bcas /

des bdag la'o //
lung brgyud kyang mdzad pa po phyin de las 'ongs pa'o //
'di gsar ma'i skor du gtogs kyang /
nyer mkho'i ched dang /
ma gcig gis kun mkhyen klong chen pa la dngos su gnang zhing /
de nyid kyi yang srid rig 'dzin pad+ma gling pa la bka' babs pa'i kun mkhyen lugs kyi nye brgyud kyang 'dres pas khyad par 'phags pa'i phyir bzhugs pa yin no //
phag mo'i skor 'di rnams sgrub sde brgyad kyi dbang du byas na /
rta mgrin gyi yum bkar gtogs pas pad+ma gsung gi gras su 'du ba nyid do //
!
//rtsa ba'i bzhi pa phrin las sgrub pa'i bka' sdod rgyal ba'i bstan srung rdo rje'i chos skyong ba'i skor rjes 'brel dang bcas pa la /
spyir 'khor 'das kyi dregs pa thams cad pho mo ma ning gi rgyud gsum du 'du zhing /
de yang gtso bor mgon po dang /
lha mo'i skor du ci rigs par 'du bas na /
'dir thog mar bstan srung kun gyi gtso bo ye shes dang las kyi mgon po'i skor las /
ye shes kyi mgon chen bka' ma rgyud kyi bka' srung legs ldan tshogs kyi bdag po dang /
mdo'i bka' srung legs ldan ljang sngon drag po gnyis su gtso bor grags pa las /
'dir rgyud mgon gyi dbang gtsang shod pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan gyi yig cha'i lugs ltar sta gon dbang bzhi drag po'i sgrol dbang dang bcas pa /
grub thob rin chen sgye nas brgyud pa g.yung ston rdo rje dpal ba'i phyag bzhes kyi dbang bskur yongs rdzogs /
zur tsho stod pa'i lugs kyi rjes gnang /
30)
sgrub yig rgyas pa las bzhi rnam rol dang /

dbang chog rnams so //
'di la dur khrod mngon par rol pa mtshon cha 'khor lo'i rgyud kyi lung tsam yod la /

'gyur med mthu stobs rnam rgyal dpal bzang po /

gter chen mchog gling pa'i thugs dam zab pa skor bdun gyi bka' srung gtso bo legs ldan tshogs kyi bdag po'i dbang chen ma hA kA la'i sgrub thabs /

32)
'di la rgyud dang man ngag gi gzhung rgya cher bzhugs pa las /

lo chen d+harma shrIs mdzad pa'i mdos kyi zin bris sgron me skor gsum zhes rdzas gsog pa'i sdom byang gsal byed sgron me /
gshom gyi lag len bca' thabs sgron me /
zur 'debs dang lag len gyi chings snang byed sgron me bcas /

yang gsang thugs sgrub /

/brgyud pa gter gsar snga ma dang 'dra /
phyag bzhi pa'i skor gter rnying cher ma byon pa ltar snang zhing phyis su bdud 'dul rdo rje dang stag sham la chos skor rgyas pa /
mi 'gyur rdo rje sogs la'ang sgrub thabs phran tshegs snang ngo //
slob dpon chen pos 'khon klu'i dbang po la gnang ba gur mgon srog gi spu gri'am mgon po phur zhabs ma'i dbang /
sgrub thabs dbang chog dang bcas pa /
brgyud pa ni /
rdo rje sems dpa'/

'khon klu'i dbang po srung ba /

dge skyabs /

/rje kun dga' mchog grub /
rje btsun grol mchog

brag stod pa lha dbang grags pa gnyis kyis zhus /
gnyis char las rje btsun sgrol mgon /
de phyin rin 'byung spyi brgyud ltar ro //
gter ston rgya pad+ma dbang phyug gis gangs bar phug mo che nas bton pa'i gur mgon gyi sgrub thabs dregs pa zil gnon /
ru mtshon 'dzugs thabs /

gur mgon gter byon 'di tsam las cher ma mthong ngo //
gter chen mchog gyur gling pa'i zab gter /
thugs rje chen po pad+ma sgyu 'phrul drwa ba'i chos sde mgon po phyag drug pa'i dbang /
sgrub thabs phrin las gter gzhung /
dbang chog
/ye rgyal nam mkha' mdzod kyi gter byon ye shes mgon po phyag drug pa'i sgrub thabs zab mo skor dgu'i thog mar phyi sgrub dang 'brel ba'i gtor dbang /
phyi sgrub gter gzhung /
dbang chog bcas /
brgyud pa ni /
snang ba mtha' yas /
thugs rje chen po /
dbang chen rta mgrin /
'phags pa klu sgrub /
o rgyan chen po /
bai ro tsa na /
mtsho rgyal /
lha sras mu rub /
mchog gyur gling pa /
des bdag la'o //
gter gsar yid bzhin 'khor lo las 'byung ba'i phyag drug pa smug mthing /
las mgon thun mong dang thun min sogs gter kha 'di la zab 'dril mang du byon par snang ba las /
dri med lhun po'i don tig tu sgrub thabs tsam dang 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug la bzhugs par grags pa tsam las mgon po 'di'i chos skor yang gter kha rnams su cher mi snang ngo //
o rgyan chen po'i bka' yi srung ma khyad par du 'phags pa zab gter kun gyi gnyer 'dzin dpal mgon ma ning srog dbang gu ru chos dbang lugs /
33)
de'i sgrub thabs gter kha gsar rnying phal mo che nas byon kyang /
rgyud sgrub thabs las tshogs bcas man ngag zab cing rgyas pa chos kyi dbang phyug
/rdor gling chos skyong bka' 'dus /
rad gling /
pad gling /
'ja' tshon snying po'i gter byon rnams su snang zhing /
de bzhi ka'i srog dbang rtsa ba gcig pa kho nar bzhugs pa dang /
gter chen 'gyur med rdo rje nas bka' srol bzhi ka gsan nas brgyud pa'i chu bo gcig tu 'du'o //
gter chen 'gyur med rdo rjes mdzad par las byang spyi 'gro las bzhi myur 'grub /
rat+na gling pas gnyal smad dge ri brag nas spyan drangs pa'i dpal mgon ma ning nag po'i srog dbang /
gtor dbang las byang gter gzhung /
sngags byang /
skong gsol chen mo /
dbang chog gnyis /
lugs 'di don gnyer mang bas zur du bkod pa'o //
brgyud pa ni /
kun bzang /
che mchog
/ma ning /
o rgyan yab yum /
lang gro lo tsA ba /
rad gling /
tshe dbang grags pa /
shAkya bkra shis /
mkhar drung /
tshe chog pa /
bkra shis dbang phyug
/karma don yod /
a rA ga
/kun shes /
bkra shis tshe brtan /
pad nor phyin gur drag ltar la /
rje gsang sngags mgon po /
de las so //
phyis byon gras gnam chos stag sham rol rdor sogs la'ang bzhugs par snang mod /
nyams len byin rlabs rgyun ma nyams pa khyad par du 'phags pa pad+ma bde chen gling pa'i gter byon srog bdud kyi skor nyid de srog dbang 'ja' tshon lugs dang ngo bo gcig pas byin rlabs kyi rgyun 'dir yang 'du'o //
de dang rjes 'brel mgon po rigs lngar grags pa las /
sku'i mgon po stag zhon gnubs lugs bka' ma dang /
zhang khrom dang /
gra nga rdo rje kun grags gter kha gnyis ldan gyi dbang /
34)
'di'i rgyud dngos grub brtan gzigs tsam rgyud 'bum kha gcig tu bzhugs /
gzhan dngos grub brtan gzigs kyi rtogs pa lnga pa /
tshar chen rin po ches mdzad pa'i skong gso rgyas pa phrin las lhun grub /
gtor chog mdor bsdus sogs kyi rgyun dang /
man ngag gi yi ge'i rigs kyi rgyun rnyed na tshol bar 'os so //
gzhan yang yar rje o rgyan gling pa'i gter byon zab cing rgyas par snang yang deng sang rgyun ma bzhugs /
bdud 'dul rdo rje'i gter phran rnal 'byor pa dung phreng can gyis bton pa'i stag zhon skor rgyas pa /
bsam gtan gling pa'i zab mo yongs 'dus su sgrub thabs man ngag srog gtad bcas zab 'dril bzhugs par snang ngo //
gsung mgon beng dmar bka' gter gnyis ldan gyi dbang /
35)
'di la'ang yig rnying gi skor mang du bzhugs mod /
bar skabs nas rgyun yod med ma 'tshal la /
phyis su bsnyen sgrub las sbyor gyi yig cha 'dra mdzad 'dug pa ni rgyud dang man ngag gi dgongs pa rang rkang tshugs min slar dpyad /
stag sham bsam gtan gling pa'i zab gter las beng dmar skor srog gtad bcas bzhugs par snang ba las gter kha gzhan du 'di'i chos skor cher ma mthong ngo //
thugs mgon gri gug mar gtogs pa gong 'khod gur dang sras mchog sogs yin la /
yon tan mgon po seng zhon gsar ma jo bo lugs kyi rjes gnang tsam las sgos bka' logs su byon pa mi snang /
phrin las mgon po trak+shad gnubs chen nas brgyud pa dwags po lugs su grags pa /

36)

37)

bka' ma spyi lugs dang /

38)

/brgyud pa grol tig rtsa ba ltar /

40)

41)

42)

43)
'di la byang gter dang rat+na'i gsang 'dus /

/brgyud pa rtsa ba dang 'dra /

44)
chos dbang /
rin chen gling pa /
las 'brel /

dang po rjes gnang brgyud rim /

rjes gnang gi ring brgyud /
slob dpon pad+ma /
pad+ma las 'brel rtsal /

/brgyud pa rtsa ba ltar ro //
nyang gter dur khrod ma mo'i rjes gnang /
45)
mnga' bdag nyang dang pad gling sogs bka' gter man ngag zab dgu bsdus pa dur khrod ma mo'i be bum la /
lha mo sh+ma shAn pa ti'i rgyud le'u bcu pa /
dkor srung nag mo sgrub rgyud le'u gnyis pa las phran dang bcas pa /

des bdag la'o //
de'ang spyir grub mtha' phyi nang chos bon sogs tshur mthong phyogs re ba'i blo rtog gi dbang du mdzad kyi don du rgyal ba'i thugs rje la phyogs lhung dang phrin las la tshad bzung bral bas phyi pa rnams 'dul ba la de'i rtags dang cha lugs 'dzin pa'i lhar sprul pas mtshon /
'jig rten gsum na dkar po'i lam gyi snang ba phra mo yan chad rgyal ba'i phrin las kyi 'jug pa yin zhing bye brag gangs can gyi ljongs 'dir dngos dang brgyud nas 'phags mchog spyan ras gzigs dang gu ru rin po che pad+mA ka ra'i gdul byar ma chud pa gcig kyang med pa'i phyir /
thang yig las /
a ya bon po lha 'bum mam rta nag gu ru rnon rtser grags pa dang /
ku sa sman pa'am khu tsha zla 'od /
bon po brag tshal sogs dmigs bsal lung bstan pa ltar de dag gis bon gter gyi phrin las gtso bor skyong ba dang /
gu ru chos dbang /
rig 'dzin rgod ldem /
rdo rje gling pa /
bstan gnyis gling pa /
phyis kyi klong gsal /
chos gling /
yongs dge sogs la'ang gter dang snyan brgyud kyi bon skor ci rigs pa byon cing phal cher deng dus kyang bon lugs la gzhan phan che ba dang /
bon gter 'ga' yang chos gter dang zung 'jug can du snang bas /
o rgyan sangs rgyas gnyis pas ris med kyi gdul bya 'dul ba la thabs mkhas kyi cho 'phrul gsang ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i rnam thar ngo mtshar rmad du byung ba'i tshul la nges pa rnyed cing gtan pa med pa'i phrin las sgo 'phar ris su ma chad par dbye ba'i rten 'byung gi slad du 'dir yang snying po tsam btsal      nas bkod pa'o //

//gnyis pa yan lag las kyi cho ga gtso bor gyur pa'i skor la gnyis /
bsnyen sgrub kyi cho ga spyi'i yan lag tu nye bar mkho ba'i skor dang /
bye brag phrin las bzhi dang 'brel ba'i las rab 'byams kyi skor ro //
dang po la'ang nang gses su dbye na bdun las /
thog mar lam gyi rtsa ba smin byed dbang dang 'brel ba'i skor la /
lo chen d+harma shrIs mdzad pa'i dbang bskur spyi'i mtshams sbyor /
lung rgyun mdzad pa po nas /
grub chen 'od gsal klong yangs /
theg mchog 'gro 'dul rdo rje /
pad+ma bshes gnyen /
kun bzang thub bstan bstan 'dzin /

'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po /
de las so //
gnam chos gzungs dbang 'grigs chags ma dang /
bka' srung spyi'i bka' gtad chags med gsung /
spyi la 'jug pa'i sku gsung thugs dbang /
zhar byung thun mong sngon 'gro'i chos bshad smin gling gter chen mdzad pa /
theg pa rim dgu'i dang po dang 'brel ba'i skyabs sdom 'bogs chog chags med mdzad pa /
lung gsang sngags mgon po las nos /
dbang gi mtshams sbyor mdor bsdus /
dbang bskur spyi la 'jug pa'i lag len rnam nges bcas /
!
gnyis pa lam gyi ngo bo bsnyen sgrub spyir gces pa'i skor la /
mnga' bdag nyang rin po che'i zab gter las tshogs spyi chings nor bu'i phreng ba dang /
man ngag gser gyi thur ma /
'di'i lung rje rin po che las zhus shing dpe rgyun dkon cing gal che bar snang bas bkod /
chos dbang rin po che'i zab gter sngags sdeb snying gzer nag po rtsa ba yan lag phyag len dang bcas pa ni bka' rgya'i gras su bzhugs /
bsnyen sgrub spyi'i gegs sel ba'i phrin las kyi lha klong gsal rdo rje snying po las byung ba'i bdud rtsi 'khyil ba'i dbang /
gter gzhung sgrub thabs /
gnam chos bdud rtsi 'khyil ba'i dbang /
sgrub thabs las tshogs bcas gter gzhung /
bla ma dgongs 'dus las bzlas brjod nus pa stobs 'byin /
bsnyen sgrub spyi la gces pa'i yi ge 'bri gung chos kyi grags pas mdzad pa /

des bdag la'o //
bskyed rim bsnyen sgrub spyi'i lag len gsal bar byed pa /
rol pa'i rdo rje'i brag gter phyag rdor dregs 'dul thems med gsang sngags spyi chings kyi skor las /
sgrub pa spyi'i khog dbub gsang sngags bcud phur /
gnad kyi zhal gdams zur bkol /
sgrub pa dang las byang spyi la gces pa'i gnad kyi zhal gdams khyad 'phags /
rtsa gsum bla rdo srog tig yongs 'dus /
rdzas mchog bya thabs lnga 'dus dwangs ma rnams dang /
bla ma dgongs 'dus las zhwa chos rin chen pad spungs /
rat+na'i rta mgrin gsang 'dus las zhwa chos rin chen 'bar ba /
rgyud dang man ngag gi gsang don lag len du bsdebs pa dam rdzas rak+ta'i sgrub tshul dang /
mkha' spyod sid+d+hu ra'i sgrub tshul gnyis po kun mkhyen bla ma 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtses mdzad pa /
dam can sde dgu'i srog 'khor dang bla rdo'i man ngag dge sbyong blo gsal rgya mtshos bsgrigs pa la so so'i gzhung mthun gyi lag len gsal byed dang nyer mkho 'ga' zhig gi kha skong byas pa /
sgrub mchod skong rdzas sogs kyi gsal byed /
rig 'dzin srog sgrub las byung ba'i dam sri mnan pa /
bdud 'dul gter byon sprul sku snying thig gi thems med sde tshan byur sri dam sri mnan pa /
sgab 'dre dam sri btsan thabs su mnan pa la ches zab pa gnam chos ma hA ba la'i bka' gtad /
de'i sgrub thabs gter gzhung dang /
lag len gsal byed /
god mnan ri rab stobs brjid bcas chags med rin po ches mdzad pa lung karma bsod nams las so //

rad gling phur pa yang gsang bla med kyi thems byang sa bcad drug pa las phran skor las sa dpyad rten 'brel gyi che ba /

dkon rgyal /

/lnga pa gson po'i don tu rten gsum rab du gnas pa'i skor la /
snga 'gyur gyi rgyud don lag len tu dril ba'i legs bshad khyad par 'phags pa rab tu gnas pa'i cho ga rgyas pa dge legs 'dod 'jo /
yon bdag bsgo ba'i gtong thun /
de nyid snying por dril ba /
rab gnas kyi lag len legs bshad rol mtsho bcas chos rgyal gter bdag gling pas mdzad pa /
rab gnas bsdus pa dge legs char 'bebs 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang pos mdzad pa /
de'i cha lag bde gshegs spyi bstod dang /
rdzas brgyad bkra shis bcas /
ar+g+ha'i cho ga ye shes rab 'bar chos sde las byung ba /
gter ma'i phyogs la bka' dgongs dang byang gter gtso bor gyur pa rab gnas kyi cho ga rgyas bsdus dang lag len gyi khyad par rnam dbye mi 'dra ba mang bas so so'i brgyud 'dzin rnams la phyag len rnam par gsal yang 'dir sdud par ma nus na /
snga 'gyur gsang ba spyi la 'jug pa ni 'dir bkod pa rnams so /

/drug pa gshin po'i don du gnas lung dpyangs thag gi man ngag la /
spyir snga 'gyur bka' ma dong sprugs lugs kyi ngan song gnas sbyong /

khyad par che ba'i cho ga gsum du yod la /

bar do'i ngo sprod thos pas rnam grol bcas smin gling gter chen gsung /

/bdun pa las rab 'byams mthar phyin par byed pa sbyin sreg gi skor la /

/gnyis pa bye brag phrin las bzhi dang 'brel ba'i las kyi tshogs rab 'byams la /
spyir las kyi ngo bo ni /
sgyu 'phrul thugs thig las /

ngo bo'i khyad par shes rab chen po'i rtsis zin pa /
byed las kyi khyad par thabs mkhas kyi mdzad pas sangs rgyas kyi phrin las yongs su rdzogs par sgrub pa'o //
nges tshig ni /

dbye na /

/rdzogs chen pa bsod nams rin chen /
rtse le rig 'dzin rnam rgyal phyin chad gong ltar ro //
dbang gnyis ni kun mkhyen bla ma rdo rje gzi brjid la dgongs brda snyan brgyud kyi bka' babs gcig 'dus su nos pa'o //

de'i dbang /

spyi khyab btags grol bklag thabs bcas so //
spyir gsar rnying gi rgyud sde gong 'og thams cad las gzungs sngags zab mo bcangs pa'i phan yon mtha' yas pa dang /
glegs bam 'chang ba'i tshul phan yon dang bcas pa /
sbyong rgyud las phung po sreg sbyong gis sdig pa sbyong ba'i skabs gnas yig gdags par gsungs pas mtshon rgyud dang rgya gzhung tshad ma rnams las btags grol gyi mtshan ma btags kyang de'i phyogs su gtogs pa ji snyed gcig mchis la /
gsar ma'i phyogs la dmigs kyis bsal ba ni so sor 'brang ma'i 'khor lo dang /
jo bo rje'i gdams ngag tu grags pa grong khyer sgrol ba'i 'khor lo /
mchod rten mthong grol gyi ras bris tsam du snang zhing /
snga 'gyur gyi phyogs 'dir btags grol gyi rgyud dang man ngag bsam gyis mi khyab par bzhugs pa las /
mtshan gzhi'i gtso bo ni kun bzang yab yum gyi dgongs pa dang /
thig le nyer lnga'i gsang sngags sogs rang byung rdo rje'i sgra rnams su snang bas 'dir bkod pa rnams rgyas bsdus 'tshams shing snying por dril ba'i man ngag phyag len rnam gsal du nges pa'i phyir don 'dus par byas kyi /
gzhan du snying thig chen mo /
byang gter dgongs pa zang thal dang /
rad gling klong gsal snying thig gi rgyud drug
/kun bzang dgongs 'dus /
zhi khro dgongs pa rang grol /
yi dam dgongs 'dus gtso bor gyur pa'i zab gter che phra phal mo che las 'byon par snang bas so so'i rjes 'brang rnams kyis phyag len 'debs pa byung na kun bzang rdo rje 'chang gi gsung de bden phyin chad dgos nges shes pa'i las su 'dug go
/des mtshon te ma bsgoms sangs rgyas kyi chos gzhan mchod rten sku gzugs 'khor lo sogs mthong grol gyi rigs /
skye bdun myang grol /
bdug pa tshor grol /
ngo sprod dang gzungs sngags thos grol /
bye ma dang mtshan ldan reg grol gyis mtshon bde myur gyi thabs du ma snga 'gyur gyi rgyud dang gdams ngag rnams las zab cing rgyas par gsungs pa las /
'dir yang thugs rje chen po'i skor sogs su rtsa ba tsam re bkod pa dang /
skabs su babs pa gter gsar thugs sgrub bar chad kun sel gyi bla ma longs sku 'gro 'dul thugs rje chen po'i skor las rigs bdag rdo rje sems dpa'i gsang sngags bklags pas grol ba dang /
pad+ma 'byung gnas la bsten nas ma bsgoms 'tshang rgya ngo mtshar chos drug gi rgyab rten pad+ma'i snying po'i rgyud bklag pa'i thabs bcas zab chos gsang ba'i bdag po 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang pos mdzad pa /
bla ma longs sku'i las tshogs /
mi 'khrugs pa'i phyag rgya mthong grol /
las kyi sems dpa' 'khor ba dong sprugs kyi dam rdzas myang grol /
rnam snang gi bye ma reg grol /
shAka thub kyi mchod rten dran grol /
snang ba mtha' yas kyi ting 'dzin sgom grol /
sman bla'i 'bab chu 'thung grol /
sems nyid ngal gso'i 'khor lo btags grol /
don yod zhags pa'i gso sbyong bslab grol /
pad+ma gtsug tor gyi bdug spos tshor grol /
rdo rje snying po'i mchod sbyin spyad grol rnams dang /
pad 'byung chos drug las /
'khor lo mthong grol dang btags grol dam rdzas myang grol bdug spos tshor grol mtshan ldan reg grol rnams kyi lag len gsal byed /
thos grol khol phyung bcas /
brgyud pa dbang dang mtshungs /
grol ba drug gi gtso bo myang grol dam rdzas kyi sgrub pa 'di nyid sgrub chen sogs phrin las lag len rgyas pa dang 'brel ba gal che mod /
deng sang sems bskyed ji ltar yang ltar snang spros bcas lag len dar srol che bas 'dir yi ges 'jigs nas ma spros te /
ku sA li'i sgrub pa po la phan par bsams nas mdo tsam bkod pa'o //
'di la gsar ma'i sngags rgyud rnams su'ang /
bris sku mthong ba don ldan sogs bris sku'i cho ga rab 'byams dang /
dri med dang jo bo'i dbu zhwa'i mchod rten mi 'khrugs pa'i gzungs rnams kyi mthong grol gzungs sngags zab mo du ma'i sgra thos pa dang /
pad+ma gtsug tor gyi sngags dung la bzlas pa'i thos grol /
de nyid kyi bdug spos tshor grol /
bdud rtsi ril bu dang gzungs sgrub kyi bum pa'i chu'i myang grol /
bye ma sogs la gzungs bcas pa dang zhal bcu gcig pa'i sngags bzlas pa po'i rdzi phyogs phog pa'i sdig pa las grol bar gsungs pa'i reg grol sogs ston pa thams cad mkhyen la thugs rje chen po dang ldan pas gang la gang 'dul rgya cher bka' bstsal pa la blo gros kyi mig ldongs shing /yid srubs kyi dpung tshogs snying la nyal ba kha cig grol ba bzhi drug sogs rnying ma kho na'i sger chos dang /
de'ang mi 'thad pa'i sgrub byed ltar snang ba bkod pa dag snang mod /
tshul 'di lta bus mtshon rang gzhan gyi grub mtha'i kha 'dzin dang /
chos brgyad snying la zhen pas 'jig rten gyi chags sdang tsam la brten /
mngon shes phra mo dang lung rigs nyi tshe ba la khungs su byas te /
chos dang gang zag tshad ldan la bdud dang bdud kyi gzhung du sgrub pa sogs ni sgrub byed rang nyid me tog mda' can gyi phrin las pa gsal bar mtshon pas de'i phyogs su gtogs pa thams cad kyang ya nga ba'i ngan song gi bshul lam chen por 'khrid pa'i ded dpon zla med pa shes par byas nas bdag legs par 'dod pa dag gis /
chos thams cad 'byung ba med pa'i mdo las /
de bzhin gshegs pas 'di skad du chos ston te /
gang zag gis gang zag la tshod bzung bar mi bya'o //
gang zag gis gang zag la tshod bzung na rma 'byung bar 'gyur te /
nga'am gzhan yang nga dang 'dra ba dag gis gang zag la tshod gzung ngo //
rigs kyi bu /
su bdag bsrung bar 'dod pa des gzhan su'i spyod pa la'ang brtag par mi bya ste /
de dag la 'di ni 'di 'dra'o zhes dpya bar mi bya'o //
zhes sogs yang yang bka' bstsal te /
sangs rgyas dang 'dra ba'i gang zag 'jig rten na dkon pas don la rton pa'i shes rab dang gzu bor gnas pa'i blo gros kyi mthus mdo rgyud tshad ldan gyi dgongs pa dang su mthun dpyad pa las /
zhal dbang yod kyis ci dgar smras pa'i rjes su 'brangs na bstan pa'i dbyen sel chen por 'gyur bar mthong bas cal sgrog tsam gyi rjes su mi rgyug pa'ang gal shin tu che bar snang ngo //
spyir btags grol sogs kyis grol ba'ang /
re zhig ngan song tsam las grol ba dang /
'khor ba las grol ba sogs dbang po dang skal pa'i khyad par mang du 'byung ba'i phyir grol ba yin na sangs rgyas thob pa lta bur go bas blor ma shong bar snang ba'ang rang nyid blo gros phur khung thug pa'i rtags yin pas snying rje ba'i gnas so //
snga 'gyur phyogs kyi bstan 'dzin phal mo che rnams kyang rtsol med a ti'i theg pa la 'og ma'i lta spyod rnams kyis do zla med pa dang /
de nyid phyogs bcu dus gsum kun tu 'byung bar dkon pa'i tshul gzengs bstod nas sgrog bzhin du rang nyid kyis yo ga gsum gyi bskyed rdzogs dang /
rdzogs chen grol ba bzhi drug gi lta spyod thams cad g.yas chung du bor nas gsar ma'i chos sde dpang mthug rnams kyi lad mo ci 'khyol la brtson pa'ang kun bzang thugs kyi bstan pa mi bzhag 'don pa'i rtags de bstan par snang ngo /

/rgyags brngan lho gter dang byang gter /

/drug pa 'phral rkyen bar chad sel ba mdos glud kyi skor la /

bsgrub bya'i las ni zhi rgyas dbang drag dang 'brel ba ci rigs pa'i nang du 'du zhing /

sngags dang /

sgrub sde chen po brgyad kyi dbang du byas na 'khor lo dang sngags sogs ni yi dam gyi rnal 'byor gang la'ang sbyar du rung ba shas che bas spyir btang ba'i las kyi yan lag dang /
mdos gtor sogs dmigs bsal 'jig rten mchod bstod kyi sde tshan du 'du bar snang ste /
mdos kyi gzhung lha 'dre stong gi dra ba'i rgyud dang /
ma mo'i rgyud sogs las rgya cher gsungs pas mtshon te shes par bya'o /

/spyi srung 'khor lo rigs gnyis so //
zhes pa'i gza' srung skor la /
pad+ma las 'brel rtsal gyis bsam yas mchod rten nag po nas bton pa'i gza' srung shin tu zab pa /
gza' srung khyad par can gter kha gzhan nas byung ba /
drang srong gi srung ba sra brtan rdo rje'i go cha /
gza'i bla rdo bca' thabs /
gza' srung nyi ma mdung gang ma rigs gnyis /
gza' lam gcod pa'i 'khor lo /
bla ma g.ya' bzang pa'i lugs kyi gza' srung 'khor lo bka' rgya ma /
gza' srung shin tu bsdus pa phyag len rgyun khyer ma /
gza' srung khyad par can lha btsun sngon mo'i gter ma thub pa dgu ldan /
'khor lo dzo ki'i man ngag
/rgod ldem nas brgyud pa'i gza' bcos zab bsdus /
rdor gling gter ma gza' srung ngag sgros ma /
gza' srung 'khor lo bcas chog btags grol karma pa rang byung rdo rje'i dag snang rnams /
klu srung rdo rje khyung chen gar dbang las 'phro gling pa'i gter ma /
sa bdag klu gnyan gyi rdzas srung /
sgrib shing byang bu gsum pa /
bla ma kha la me 'bar gyi gter ma rgyal srung 'khor lo /
rgyal srung nya mchu ma zab pa'i gdams pa /
rgyal po shi 'dre sogs srung mdud kyis srung ba /
rgyal gdon sogs bar chad kyis mi tshugs pa'i za yig dum pa rgya'i gter ma /
grol tig gi dbang chen dregs pa kun 'dul las mtha' rgyal bsen srung ba mdud chog
/gnam chos dag snang gnam lcags sdig pa'i srog mdud /
btsan srung thogs chog 'khor lo las 'brel gter ma /
sngags mdud legs ldan rje'i phyag len /
btsan gyi bla rdo gtod la bzung ba chos dbang gter ma /
btsan srung rta mgo ma /
rtil srung hrIHkhog ma /
gson 'dre kha chings zab mo rig 'dzin ngag gi dbang po las brgyud pa /
gshed srung thod pa'i gur khang dam brgya'i man ngag gnubs kyi mgul khug ma /
sri zlog 'khor lo 'bar ba'i tsakra bca' thabs sprul sku nam mkha' brgya byin phyag len ma /
khams pa me zor gyi gter ma kag srung rgya gram ma /
sgrib shing nag po kun thub gu ru jo tshe sogs gter rnying mang po las byung ba /
'dre gdon thams cad bskrad cing srung ba'i rdzas sngags grub thob dmar po'i gter ma /
ye shes spyan gyi tsakra /
ma ti'i bdud 'dul drag mo las lba ba'i srung 'khor /
gnyid srung ba'i man ngag khyad par can /
chang srung bdud rtsi'i rgya mtsho /
chang srung lha btsun sngon mo'i gdams pa /
sris rkun srung ba rnying ma bka' ma'i man ngag
/so srin gyi nad srung ba'i sngags a tsar+Ya dmar po'i gdams pa /
so srung 'khor lo gru chod ma /
nyang gter grib dang mi gtsang ba srung ba'i 'khor lo /
ngag srung 'grol gyi gdams pa rad gling gter ma /
bsam gtan nyal chog gi rdzogs chen lugs kyi 'khor lo mtshan nyi shu rtsa gcig pa gter ston sbur po bya thul dang rdor gling pad gling sogs kyi gter kha las byung ba /
'go ba'i lha lnga mi dgyes pa las srung ba'i 'khor lo dbu ru shAka 'od gter ma /
srog lus dbang thang klung gta' la dgra dar ba las srung ba bskyed pa bzhi ldan gyi 'khor lo sprul sku tshe brtan rgyal mtshan gyi gter ma bcas so //
srung ba'i skor 'di rnams rje bla mas lung rgyun yongs 'dzin ci rigs pa las gsan cing phyogs gcig tu bsdud par mdzad pa las kho bos thos pa'o /
!
/gnyis pa 'byung bzhi'i 'jigs pa srung ba'i skor la /
kun skyong gling pa'i gter ma sa g.yos srung ba sogs sa chu me rlung bzhi'i 'jigs pa srung ba zab bsdus /
chos dbang gter byon sogs shwa 'od srung ba'i chu sgyur zab btus /
'jigs med gling pa'i dag snang gru gzings mi log pa'i srung ba thugs rje byams pa'i man ngag 'gro ba'i srog 'dzin /
gter gsar thugs sgrub las 'byung bzhi'i 'jigs srung phyogs bsdus bltas chog tu bsdebs pa rnams so /

dus ma yin pa'i 'chi ba ste 'jigs pa chen po brgyad du gsungs pas mtshon mi mthun cing mi 'dod pa'i nye bar 'tshe ba mtha' dag yin la /

/srung zlog las rim khyer bde bdud 'joms rdo rje'i go mtshon /
zlog byang rgyas pa /
thugs sgrub cha lag bar chad sel ba'i lha bzhi las nang bdud bzhi'i bar chad sel ba mi g.yo ba rigs bzhi'i dbang sgrub thabs bdud bzhi zil gnon gter gzhung tshang ba /dbang chog bai DUr+Ya'i chu rgyun /

/gnyis pa nad zhi ba'i skor la /

/pad gling kun bzang dgongs 'dus cha lag ri khrod ma'i sgrub thabs nyon mongs nad 'joms /

lo rgyus mdos chog dang bcas pa /

'brog mi dpal ye'i rnam 'phrul gro shul bde chen gling pa'i zab gter gso dpyad 'chi med tshe bum   
'di lung rgyun tsam snang mod brgyud pa mi gsal yang sman sbyor phal cher lag len can yin skad    gnam chos gter byon dang chags med kyis mdzad pa'i khyi smyon bcos thabs /
mid 'byar gyi rigs bcos thabs sngags dang me btsa' rdzas sbyor gyi skor 'chi ba mal nas slong byed gnam chos mi 'gyur rdo rjes mdzad pa /

klong gsal rdo rje snying po las seng ge sgra'i dbang /
de'i sgrub thabs dang dbang chog
/srung ma klu'i cho ga gter gzhung /

drag sbyong sdig pa khar 'jug

gdon khrol ngar glud kyi cho ga kha skong sogs dang bcas pa rnams so /

/bzhi pa grib dang mi gtsang ba gtsor gyur zhi ba'i skor la /
snga 'gyur bka' ma bi ma la'i lugs kyi rnam 'joms dkar po   klong gsal zab gter bi ma'i rgyud sde bzhi'i skor gyi rnam 'joms dkar po'ang 'di dang shin tu mthun pas bka' gter gnyis ldan no    bka' brgyud kaM tshang la bka' babs pa'i dbang /

48)

49)
'di dag gsar ma'i phyogs yin yang /
'dod bum du nyer mkho'i dbang gis bzhag par snang ngo //
rnam 'joms mthing ga'i sgrub thabs khrus chog dang bcas pa bdud rtsi'i snying po can smin gling gter chen gsung mkhan chen o DI ya nas nag 'gros su spel ba /
'di pad gling nor rgyam dang 'brel bar bzhed 'dug
/gnam chos rnam 'joms ljang gu'i dbang /
gter gzhung /
chos lugs mi gtsang ba'i nyes sel /

brgyud 'debs gter gsung /
las byang dang dbang bskur bklag chog tu bkod pa /
klong gsal snying po'i gter byon rnam 'joms dkar po'i dbang /

grwa mngon dbang phyug 'bar gyi gter byon 'khon sbyong ba'i man ngag khyad par can /

brgyud pa mnga' bdag nyid nas rim par brgyud pad+ma gar dbang phyin chad seng gdong bka' bcu ltar drang chog
/gu ru chos dbang gter byon khro mo sme brtsegs kyi sgrub thabs las tshogs dang bcas pa /
bla ma gsang 'dus cha lag mkha' 'gro grib sel bklag chog tu bkod pa /
khro bo sme brtsegs zhal gcig phyag gnyis pa'i khrus chog 'gyur med rdo rjes mdzad pa   'di snga 'gyur gyi phyogs su snang yang khungs tshol dgos    'gro 'dul gling pa shes rab 'od zer gyi zab gter grol tig gi cha lag khro bo sme brtsegs kyi sgrub thabs dam      grib nyes pa kun sel /
de'i sgrub thabs las tshogs gnas khang gi nyams grib zhi ba dang bskyed rim nyams grib sel byed sogs bcas /
'ja' tshon gter byon ma ning zhi ba'i las tshogs mkha' 'gro grib sel bklag chog tu bkod pa /
klong gsal rdo rje snying po las khro bo sme brtsegs dang mkha' 'gro sme brtsegs kyi dbang /
de gnyis kyi sgrub thabs gter gzhung /
ye shes rab 'bar las grib dang mi gtsang ba sel ba'i thabs /
khro bo sme brtsegs sgo nas rnal 'byor pa rang gi grib sel ba'i cho ga
/gzhan gyi nyams grib sel byed /

e ne ring nub dgon pa mkhas grub ngag dbang rdo rje'i gter ma sme ba brtsegs pa'i dbang /
sgrub thabs dbang bskur bcas gter gzhung /

o rgyan pad+ma /
ye shes mtsho rgyal /
ngag dbang rdo rje /

chos dbyings bde chen mtsho mo /
'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po'i zhal snga nas bdag la'o //
rig 'dzin tshe dbang nor bus mdzad pa'i phag mo sme brtsegs kyi sgom bzlas /
mchog gling zab gter thugs sgrub bar chad kun sel gyi cha lag thun mong nyams grib kyi bar chad sel ba khro rgyal sme ba brtsegs pa'i dbang /
sgrub thabs gter gzhung tshang ba /
dbang chog zla shel bdud rtsi'i chu rgyun /
sbyin sreg rgyal dbang theg mchog rdo rjes mdzad pa /
sbyin sreg gi lung rgyun rgyal dbang nyid nas rje dbon chos dbang sprul sku
/de las so //
gzhan yang chos dbang rin po che'i zab gter rnam 'joms gnam skas ma'i byin rlabs sgrub skor bcas dang /
rdor gling dang /

sme brtsegs kyi khrus chog sogs snga phyi'i zab gter ci rigs pa'ang mchis so /

/lnga pa byad phur rbod gtong zhi ba'i skor la /

/drug pa snod bcud kyi nyes pa zhi ba'i skor la /
bla ma dgongs 'dus gzhan don las tshogs kyi skor drug las nyes pa kun sel byin rlabs sgron me /

/de'i lag len zin bris gter dbon o rgyan lhun grub kyis mdzad pa /

/byang gter mnga' dbang rin chen 'bar ba'i cha lag bum gter yid bzhin bcas chog

rig 'dzin thugs mchog rdo rje'i zab gter rtsa gsum dbang chen 'dus pa'i cha lag bkra shis gter sgrub 'dod dgu'i bang mdzod las byang bde legs kun 'byung gter gzhung /

/brgyud pa gong gi sgrol dkar sogs dang mtshungs /

'chi med grub pa'i rig 'dzin legs ldan bdud 'joms rdo rje la gu ru rin po ches dngos su bstsal pa tshe'i dngos grub sgrub pa'i man ngag nam mkha' zas su za ba'i gdams pa rtsa ba /

klong gsal rdo rje snying po las rgyal yum rnam par rgyal ma'i rjes gnang dang tshe dbang /

'phags ma'i snying thig gi cha lag rnam par rgyal ma'i stong mchod cho ga
/byang gter snying mdzod nas byon pa'i 'chi bdag zlog byed stobs chen gyad kyi 'khor lo'i chog khrigs rig 'dzin pad+ma phrin las kyis mdzad pa //

/'di'i lung rgyun bar ma chad par byung yang brgyud pa nges gsal mi snang /

'ja' tshon ma ning zhi ba'i las tshogs mkha' 'gro sun zlog gi las 'grigs /

bka' brgyad gsang rdzogs kyi cha lag chu sbyin stong zlog
/'chi bslu bsdus pa slob dpon gsung /

rtags brgyad 'bul ba /

rdzas brgyad 'bul ba /
klong gsal dang mchog gling gter byon gzhir byas pa'i tshe thar gtang thabs phan bde'i snying po bcas /
!
gnyis pa yon tan thams cad kyi rtsa ba shes rab rgyas par byed pa'i skor la /
nyang gter drag po dmar chen las byung ba'i 'jam dpal sgos sgrub /
chos dbang bla ma gsang 'dus las /
blo ldan mchog sred kyi sgos sgrub /
rdor gling lta ba klong yangs kyi cha lag 'jam dpal dmar ser blo yi mun sel /
sangs gling bla ma dgongs 'dus chos sde 'jam dbyangs dmar ser rjes gnang /
shes rab ral gri gter gzhung rjes gnang cho ga
/mnga' ris paN chen gyi rig 'dzin yongs 'dus chos sde 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi thugs sgrub /
mchog gling thugs sgrub bar chad kun sel las bla ma smra ba'i seng ge'i dbang /
sgrub thabs rgyun khyer gter ston nyid mdzad /
phrin las dbang bskur las tshogs dang bcas pa'i gsal byed blo gros kha 'byed /
rad gling gter phran phag dkar shes rab gsal byed /
rat+na gling pas bsam yas byang chub chen po'i sku rgyab nas gdan drangs pa'i lha mo dbyangs can ma'i sgrub thabs /
bstod pa gter ston nyid mdzad /
brgyud pa dpal yul spyi 'gro'o //
'gro 'dul shes rab 'od zer gyi gter phran shes rab blo 'phel mi brjed gzungs thob /
de nyid kyi dgongs gter rdo rje dbyangs can ma'i sgrub thabs blo gros gsal byed /
dregs 'joms zhi sgrub 'jam dbyangs dmar ser /
klong gsal rdo rje snying po las phag dkar shes rab gsal byed kyi dbang /
gter gzhung rtsa ba /
sgrub thabs dbang chog dang bcas pa /
kun mkhyen bla ma 'od gsal sprul pa'i rdo rje'i zab mo dgongs pa'i gter gyi chos sde rdo rje rnal 'byor ma rigs lnga las phag dkar shes rab gsal byed rtsa gzhung /
phrin las dang rgyun khyer me mchod rje nyid kyi ljags bsgrigs /
dbang chog ye shes snang ba'i rgyan /
brgyud pa ni /
kun tu bzang po /
rdo rje rnal 'byor ma /
gu ru yab yum /

50)

51)
sgrub thabs las tshogs bcas kyi gzhung dam pas mdzad pa /

drang srong nyi ma'i shing rta /

52)
sgrub thabs dang bstod pa bram ze phur bu dang las sbyor rtsa ba drang srong mngon shes can gyis mdzad pa /

/gsum pa yon tan thams cad kyi gzhi bsod nams dang dpal 'byor longs spyod snyan grags rgyas par byed pa'i skor la /

53)
tshar chen yab sras kyis bsgrigs pa'i rnam sras be bum las byung ba'i lo rgyus nas dam tshig bstan pa'i bar yig rnying tshang ba bzhugs /

55)

56)
gnod sbyin dbyug to can gyi rgyud dang /
tshe sgrub kyi gsal byed bi ma las mdzad pa khro phu lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyi zab gter sgrub thabs dgos 'dod kun 'byung sogs yig rnying dang bsnyen sgrub las sbyor rjes gnang bcas gnyags dbon rin po ches mdzad pa /

tshar chen /

bsod nams mchog grub /
mkhyen rab byams pa man chad ser chen ltar ro //
rat+na'i rta mgrin gsang 'dus kyi bka' srung rnam sras mdung dmar can rta bdag brgyad kyis bskor ba'i dbang /
phrin las dbang chog dang bcas pa /
pad gling bla ma nor bu rgya mtsho las byung ba'i rnam sras yang gsang bla med kyi dbang /
dbang chog las byang las tshogs kyi skor sogs gter gzhung tshang ba /
srung ma'i phrin las /
dngos grub rol mtsho'i dkyus su bkod pa'ang phyi ma 'di gnyis dang mthun pa'o //
'di'i nang sgrub dang mdung dmar can gyi skor rnams gtso bor dbang gi las kyi lhar rtogs shing /
gsang sgrub ni drag po'i las sbyor gyi lha yin na'ang /
rnam sras kyi skor rnams phyogs gcig tu 'brel ba'i slad 'dir bkod pa'o //
rnam sras mdung dmar skor sangs gling dang rdor gling rnams la'ang bzhugs par snang ngo //
gu ru chos kyi dbang phyug gi gter byon pad+ma g.yang 'bum yid bzhin nor bu smon dang bkra shis 'brel chags bcas /

rtogs ldan dkon mchog rgyal mtshan /
rdo rje gzi brjid /

lo chen bai ro dang ska ba dpal brtsegs zung 'jug gi rnam 'phrul bshes gnyen grwa ston chen pos bsam yas nas bton pa'i dzaM la dmar po gsung gi sgrub pa'i dbang /

rat+na'i klong gsal gyi cha lag phyi dzaM ser /

las gzhung dngos grub char 'bebs /

bzhi pa lo tog 'bras bu rgyas byed kyi skor la /
char 'bebs kyi man ngag bka' gter gyi gdams pa zab par grags pa mtha' yas pa las /
dregs 'dul gyi las tshogs dang 'brel ba'i char 'bebs zab mo phyag bzhes ma ni klu chog gdengs can bdud rtsir gsal ba ltar dang /
'dir pad gling bla ma nor bu rgya mtsho'i cha lag char 'bebs pa'i gdams pa rgya nag chu 'khor klu sgrub lugs phyag len ma /
Dom+bi lugs kyi char 'bebs zhal shes dang bcas pa /
byang gter zhing gi lud sbyor dang byi ba srung ba /
char 'bebs drag rdzas phyag bzhes ma /
gnam chos sa snying dbang /

dgongs gter klu rgyal dga' bo'i bka' gtad /
de'i sgrub thabs /
klu mchod chags med gsung /

de'i gsal byed dang gsol kha g.yang skyabs sbrags ma chags med gsung /
bla ma dgongs 'dus char 'bebs bdud rtsi bum chung dang 'ja' tshon gter ma sogs zab bsdus char 'bebs cho ga
/char 'bebs stabs bde bdud rtsi sprin chen /
sprin chen mdo'i don bsdus smon lam bden stobs /
'bu srin gdug pa kha bsgyur gyi bsang yig
/gnod pa zhi byed bsang bsdus gnyis /

spring yig
/zhing lha bstod pa'i mchod gsol rnams chags med kyis mdzad pa /
gzhan yang bka' brgyad rang shar gyi char 'bebs yongs rdzogs /
byang gter thugs sgrub dang bla ma dgongs 'dus kyi lo tog phan byed skor /

de'i yig chung gser gyi lde'u mig
/gter bum gyi lag len gsal byed /
rig 'dzin thugs kyi rdo rje'i dgongs gter seng ge sgra'i dbang /

lo glud gtang thabs 'gong po gru 'ded /

de'i tshogs mchod /

lung rgyun mdzad pa po las nos /
yang gong gi sha za mched gsum ltar ded kyang chog
/lo tog la phan pa'i gdams ngag bdud rtsi'i snying po rje bla ma rin po ches mdzad pa /
lo tog rgyas pa'i smon lam grub chen thang rgyal gsung byin rlabs can /
lo legs sad ser zhi ba'i smon lam chags med gsung bcas /

lnga pa yon tan gyi snod du gyur pa rigs rgyud rgyas par byed pa la /

zab gter so so'i las phran las byung ba'ang mang du snang rung sdud par ma nus la /
'dir chos dbang gsang 'dus thems med kyi skor du gtogs pa lha bu btson 'dzin gyi srung ba bri thabs /

/drug pa yon tan thams cad kyi 'byung gnas sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa rin po che rgyas byed kyi skor la /
gter chen sangs rgyas gling pa'i zab gter las byon pa thub dbang gnas brtan bcu drug gi rjes gnang /
cho ga mchod pa'i sprin phung dang rjes gnang gi yi ge gar dbang zhig po gling pas mdzad pa /
gnas brtan mchod chog snying por dril ba kun gzigs mkhyen brtse'i dbang pos mdzad pa /
'ja' tshon zab gter 'gro 'dul bstan pa rgyas pa'i sAts+tsha'i lag len /
klong gsal rdo rje snying po las /
rje btsun byams pa mgon po'i dbang /
byams pa'i sgrub thabs dbang chog dang bcas pa lung rtogs bcud spel /
gnam chos las byung ba'i thub dbang gnas brtan 'khor bcas kyi dbang /
sgrub thabs las tshogs dbang dang bcas pa gter gzhung /
dbang sgrub dang dbang bshad chags med kyis mdzad pa /
dge 'dun 'du ba'i 'khor lo bri thabs thems med las byung ba /
mkhas grub karma chags med kyi gsung sprul karma bde chen snying pos mdzad pa rtsa gsum 'dus pa'i sgrub mchod nor bu bsam 'phel /
lung rgyun mdzad pa po nas gcod bla karma phrin las /
bde chen sprul sku
/dkon mchog rgyal mtshan /
rje mkhyen brtse las so //
mang dge rdo rje 'chang dge legs yar 'phel gyis mdzad pa'i thub chog gser zhun snying po zin bris bcas lung rgyun mdzad pa po nas /
mkhan po blo bzang rnam rgyal /
mkhan bla ma karma bkra shis 'od zer las nos /
'di rgyas pa'i las kho nar ma nges kyang phan yon la bsams nas zhar byung bzhag pa'o /

/bdun pa mthar thug nyams rtogs kyi ye shes rgyas par byed pa ni /
snga phyir bskyed rdzogs kyi gdams zab ji snyed cig 'byung ba rnams so /

/las 'brel zab gter lha chen dbang phyug chen po'i rjes gnang /
59)
'di'i rgyud dang sgrub thabs las tshogs sogs rags rim gyi rgyun tsam bzhugs snang /

/thugs rje chen po pad+ma sgyu 'phrul drwa ba'i bka' srung lha chen bka' gtad /

/rat+na'i klong gsal snying thig bka' srung lha chen rlung zhags /
bdud 'dul dang gnam chos sogs zab par grags pa rnams kyi dbang lung gi rgyun ci rigs bzhugs par snang zhing /
spyir rong zom pa chen po'i las byed rlung zhon ma'i skor ngo mtshar can dang /
jo bo rje la slob dpon rin po ches gnang bar grags pa'i mos pa rnam bzhi'i dbang sdud /
mchims rdo rje sprel chung gi skye mtha' gu ru jo tshe'i dbang phyug nag po'i dbang sdud las kyi 'khor lo /
gnyal pa jo sras kyi dbang sdud nor bu gcig pa /
gu ru ye shes khyung grags kyi spos dkar dang sbrang rtsis snang ba dbang sdud sogs gter phran rigs mang du bzhugs par snang na'ang rgyun yod med ma 'tshal la /
rat+na'i rta gsang dang /
'ja' tshon ma ning gi las tshogs bzo rig pa'i skor dang /
dgongs 'dus 'byung ba dbang sdud grub rtags kyi skor sogs kyang skabs 'dir 'du ba yin no //
mthar thug rlung sems dbang du bsdu ba ni gong 'og tu rdzogs rim zab mo'i rnal 'byor ji snyed cig 'byung ba rnams so //
dbang dang rgyas pa'i lha rnam sras dang dzam la'i skor sogs sgrub sde chen po brgyad du bsdu ba'i tshe rin po che'i rigs kyi nges pas bdud rtsi yon tan gyi phyogs su gtogs par byas kyang mi 'gal zhing /
nang gses su dzam dmar dang lha chen sogs pad+ma gsung gi rigs su snang mod /
spyir btang gnod sbyin dang dregs pa'i sde dpon chen po'i tshul du ston pa 'jig rten mchod bstod kyi nang du 'du ba'ang yin no /

'di la 'khor lo bco brgyad tsam gyi dpe'u ris dang gnad gdams zhal shes thun min bzhugs pa de dag zhib cha ma byung na dpe tsam gyis go mi chod par snang yang dpe lung gi rgyun tsam la bsams nas bkod pa mkhyen ldan dag gis 'khor lo zhal shes rtsad gcod par zhu /

gnyis pa mngon spyod bye brag tu sgrub pa ni /
'jam dpal gshin rje'i man ngag las /
srung ba rdo rje'i mkhar du gzhug :
zlog pa byad ma rang gshed 'bebs :
bsad pa nyams pa bdun rgyud gcod :
mtha' sdud 'byung ba bzhi la gtad :
ces srung zlog bsad mnan mtha' sdud de bzhir 'du ba las /
dang po srung ba ni /
spyir rdzas dang 'khrul 'khor sogs kyi sgo nas srung ba dang /
bye brag yi dam so so dang 'brel ba'i srung ba'i rim pa ji snyed cig bkod zin pas /
'dir sa bcad tsam du chos dbang rin po che'i zab gter byad ma 'bum thub kyi srung 'khor lag len dang bcas pa /
rang phyogs srung ba gnubs lugs bka' ma a pa rA dzi ta'i rtsod rgyal rdo 'khor man ngag dang bcas pa lab ston nam mkha' rin chen gyis bsgrigs pa /
lung brgyud mdzad pa po nas rim par brgyud /
sga rje bla ma pad+ma lhun grub /
pad+ma chos 'phel /
gsang sngags mgon po las so //
rat+na'i gter phran mnyam gnyis rtsal 'gran chings gsum gyi gdams pa /
gnubs kyi man ngag rtsod rgyal ga kha ltag sprod /
dbang phyug chen po la bsten pa'i btsan po kha chings rnams /
