gnyis pa zlog pa'i skor /
drag phur gshed skor sogs so so'i chos sde dang 'brel pa khyer bde gtsor gyur kha shas ni de dag gi dkyus su bkod zin /
'dir nyer mkho phra mo'i rigs la /
chags med kyis mdzad pa'i sgrub pa bka' brgyad gtor zlog khro rol shin tu bsdus pa dang /
dgra chos dgra bgegs tshar gcod /
gter chen mchog gyur gling pa'i zab gter bod khams bde thabs chos bcu'i nang tshan /
nam mkha' mdzod kyi lho phyogs gshin rje'i rba dong nas spyan drangs pa'i bstan pa srung ba'i chos bzhi zhes gshin rje 'jigs byed rol pa /
rta mgrin bskal pa'i me phung /
phur pa khro rgyal stobs 'dus /
mgon po gnam lcags thog mda' rnams kyi gzhung /
mgon po'i bka' gtad /
snga ma gsum la dbang zur du mi bzhugs shing zab bdun gyi rno so yin par gsungs /
yang zlog phra mo'i skor la /
gnub lugs 'jam dpal gshin rje'i gshed mthu stobs dregs pa'i rgyal po la bsten pa'i srung zlog bsad mnan rgyun gyi rnal 'byor dbang po'i sdes mdzad pa /

yang zlog gnubs kyi gong khug ma /

mkha' 'gro'i yang zlog

gnubs lugs yang zlog a thung nag po /
gu ru pad+ma sid+d+his mdzad pa'i yang zlog sngags kyi shan pa /
shrI siM ha'i yang zlog za yig bka' rgya ma /

karma bsod nams las nos so //
yang zlog rgyun khyer smin gter dang chos kyi 'byung gnas kyis mdzad pa zhal shes bcas /
bde gling gter byon yang zlog rdo rje pha lam 'khor lo bri yig bcas pa dang /
de'i nyams len rig 'dzin tshe dbang nor bus mdzad pa /
des mdzad pa'i rgyun khyer /

gter kha gsum 'dus yang zlog rdo rje pha lam gyi srung zlog bsad pa'i lag len bklag chog tu bkod pa /
nyer mkho'i byang bcas /

gshin rje'i gshed /
'jam dpal bshes gnyen /
gtsug lag dpal dge
/gter ston nas rim par /
byang bdag yab sras /
yol mo ba /
zur chen /
lnga pa /
gter chen /
blo gros chos 'phel /
shes rab 'byung gnas /
de sras ngag dbang nor bu /
sman sgom kun dga' dpal ldan /
'ba' ra ba kun bzang chos dbyings rdo rje /
dpa' bo gtsug lag chos rgyal /
pad sprul pad dbang /
sgrol ston 'jam dbyangs /
rje mkhyen brtse'i zhal las so //
yang bka' gter gnyis ldan ltar na /
legs ldan rje nas rim par brgyud /
dpon slob za lung pa /
sa skya pa kun dga' blo gros /
rin chen rgyal mtshan /
kun dga' bkra shis /
byams pa smon lam grags pa /
mkhyen brtse rin po che'o //
rat+na'i gter byon gtad zlog man ngag rgyal po bka' rgya ma /
gnubs lugs urmo'i man ngag gtad zlog sbal pa dkar nag gi sbyor ba /
gtad srung dang nye 'byed dpe'u ris /
zhar byung gtad rul dmar po khyung po rnal 'byor gyi man ngag
/shin tu zab pa'i man ngag 'dun gros ngan pa chu bsgyur bka' gter zung 'jug byang pa'i lugs /
'dun bshigs pad gnubs thun mong lugs 'bri gung phyag bzhes ma /
cha gsum bsngo tshul /
gdams phran kha shas bcas /
mi kha zlog pa'i rigs la /
thugs rje chen po la bsten pa chags med gsung /
'jam dpal gshin rje'i las mtha' rtsod dang mi kha zlog pa stag sham gter ma /
nyang gter mi kha dgra zlog
/ye 'bar las smra ngan mi kha'i zlog pa phrin las rlung gi 'khor lo /
mi kha thal rdeb khyung grags rdo rje'i gter ma /
dbang phyug chen pos mi kha zlog pa gnubs kyi u pa de sha
/mi kha dgra bsgyur gyi gto a ya bon po lha 'bum gyi gter ma /
brgyud pa gong gi btsan mdos dang 'dra /
gter gsar thugs sgrub 'jam dpal pha rol rgol 'joms las tshogs mi kha srung zlog mnan pa sogs phyogs bsdus /
ltas ngan zlog pa'i man ngag
/than zlog shing byang /
stag sham yi dam dgongs 'dus khyung sgrub las mtha' ltas ngan brgyad cu'i zlog mdos bcas /
!
gsum pa bsad pa la /
yi dam so so dang 'brel ba ni gong du bkod zin /
gzhan man ngag zab mor grags pa mtha' yas pa las 'dir bka' ma gnubs lugs gshin rje king kang nag po'i bsad pa myur mgyogs stag byang ma shin tu zab pa'i phyag len zin bris dgra dpung srog 'phrog sngags byang gud sbas /
mkhyen dgongs dmod bcol /
zhal shes /
dpe'u ris bcas /
brgyud pa ni /
lnga pa chen po nas /
'jam dbyangs grags pa /
byang gling slob dpon nas rim par /
'jigs med bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan /
sgam po rdo rje /
tshe brtan rgyal po /
rig pa'i rdo rje /
rdo rje gzi brjid /
des so //
nye brgyud ni /
chos kyi grags pa'i ye shes skus rjes su bzung pa pad+ma dgyes pa /
sa man+ta b+ha dra /
zla ba tshe brtan rgyal po man 'dra /
bla ma grum pa dang yon bdag nag po mkhar gnyis kyis spa gro skyer chu lha khang nas bton pa'i gza' bdud drag sngags kyis dgra bo bar snang hom khung du bsad pa'i gdams skor lo rgyus /
sgrub thabs /
las mtha' dang bcas pa /
grub thob me long rdo rje la rA hu las dngos su phul pa zhal gdams gnad kyi shog dril lho brag mkho mthing gi brag la gter du sbas pa bla ma phyag rdor bas bton pa /
drang srong khyab mjug gi las spu gri nag po pra dun rtse'i ka zhu nas sngags pa dbang chen gyis bton pa /
a tsar+Ya grags pa'i ye shes kyis gdams pa ngan sngags mu stegs rde'u nag po dge bshes dbang shAka gter ma /
rA hu la dang re ma ti gnyis kyi cho 'phrul khyad 'phags gter ston shes rab me 'bar gyi gter ma /
gza'i rjes gcod dang phyi lam bcad pa snying ri lugs khams pa khra mos bsam yas nas bton pa /
drang srong chig shur gyi bsnyen sgrub las gsum gyi lag khrid dbang po'i sdes mdzad pa bcas 'di rigs deng sang las 'brel gza' pod kyi dkyus la bzhugs pas lung rgyun kyang de dang mtshungs la kho bos rje bla ma 'jam            dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i zhal las so //
gza' bdud bar snang hom khung ma'i sger brgyud ni /
rdo rje 'chang /
sangs rgyas rin chen snying po /
thub dbang /
shrI sing+ha /
gu ru rin po che /
mtsho rgyal /
khri srong /
gter ston bla ma grum dang yon bdag nag po mkhar /
gnubs ban ston pa /
dge bshes gnyan chad pa /
'dar ston pa /
gnyos 'bum khri ston pa /
skyogs bya zhu can /
rat+ne shwa ra /
gsang sngags rdo rje /
bkra shis stobs rgyal /
ngag gi dbang po /
chos dbyings rang grol /
rdo rje thogs med sogs nas rim par brgyud /
rje bla ma mkhyen brtse'i dbang po'i zhal snga nas so //
de la spyir srung zlog bsad gsum so sor phyi mtshan bcas rdzas la gtso bor brten pa dang /
nang mtshan bcas ting nge 'dzin kho na las grub pa dang /
gsang ba mtshan med de kho na nyid kyi lta bas rgyas 'debs pa'i tshul rgya cher gsungs so /
!
/bzhi pa mtha' sdud la /
sngags sdeb las /
cha gsum dag tu bgo ba ni :
mnan sreg 'phang ba'i las gsum yin :
zhes srung ba'i mtha' sdud mnan pa /
zlog pa'i mtha' sdud 'phang ba /
bsad pa'i mtha' sdud sreg pa ste gsum du gsungs pa nyid 'byung ba bzhi'i sbyor bas bsdus pa yin te /
dang po sa la mnan pa'i las ni /
gyim shang bka' gter gyi gzhung so sor bshad pa dang /
gtad gzhung rnams las rgya cher gsungs pa'i sa gtad kyi skor /
yi dam tha dad pa dang 'brel ba'i mnan pa'i las mtha' ji snyed cig byung ba sogs las /
'dir dgra bo mnan pa'i las drag sngags bdag po rgya zhang khrom gyi gter ma /
gshin rje gshed kyi king kang dmar po rtsa gzhung /
de'i gsal byed bka' gter gnyis ldan gyi las byang byang bdag gis mdzad pa dmod byang bcas /

gshin rje gshed dmar /
'jam dpal bshes gnyen /
o rgyan /

pad+ma dbang /

des bdag la'o //
king dmar gyi lag len gnad 'dril dge sbyong blo gsal rgya mtshos mdzad pa /
king dmar rlung sgrub khrigs chags ma bstan dgra 'joms byed zhig gling mdzad pa /
lung de nyid nas sog zlog pa phyin 'og gi king nag dang 'dra /
de'i lag len zhal shes karma kun mkhyen mdzad pa /
king dmar rlung sgrub las byang 'bri gung chos kyi grags pas mdzad pa /
lung rgyun mdzad pa po nas /
dkon mchog lhun grub /
blo mchog rdo rje /
lnga pa chen po phyin chad byang lugs dang 'dra /
king dmar gang la'ang sbyar du rung ba'i tshogs mchod nyung ngu chags med mdzad pa /
gnam chos sgrub thabs rgya mtsho las byung ba'i king dmar rigs bco lnga las king kang dmar byed kyi dbang /
sgrub thabs gter gzhung /
king nag pha rol rgol 'joms bka' gter gnyis ldan gyi lag len gsal byed tshogs mchod dang bcas pa sog zlog pa blo gros rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa /
lung mdzad pa po nas rim par brgyud /
rig 'dzin chen po /
bstan pa'i nyin byed /
rta mgrin mgon po /
tshe ring phun tshogs /
bla ma nor bu /
karma bsod nams /
de las so //
king nag las gzhung phrin las 'dod 'jo dang /
srung zlog dgra chings mdor bsdus glang ru ma'i rgyun khyer zab gsang gnad 'dril tshe dbang kun khyab kyis mdzad pa /
kun khyab kyi gsung tshan rnams mdzad pa po nas /
karma theg mchog
/gu ru ma Ni /
pad dkar sprul sku dpal ldan rdo rje /
karma nges don dpal bzang /
rje rin po che mkhyen brtse'i zhal las nos so //
pha rol rgol 'joms man ngag gnad dril gyi zin bris /
bgegs mnan pa'i sbyor ba byang gter phur pa drag sngags spu gri'i sri chung bcu gsum mnan thabs lag len dang bcas pa /
byang gter thugs sgrub las tshogs bcu gnyis pa 'gong po ar gtad gter gzhung /
ar gtad kyi man ngag lag len rnam gsal du bkod pa /
yi dam spyi la sbyar du rung ba'i dgra bgegs mnan pa'i las rim bcas /
!
gnyis pa chu la gtad pa ni /
bla ma mnga' bdag chen po /
las 'brel /
sangs gling sogs kyi gtad khrom skor zab rgyas mtha' yas pa las /
'dir sa bcad tsam du las 'brel gyi phyag rdor dregs 'dul las mtha' thems med gtad khrom gyi gzhung lag len dang bcas pa tsam zhig bkod do /
!
/gsum pa me la bsregs pa las drag po'i sbyin sreg gi cho ga ni /
spyi dang bye brag pa ci rigs pa bkod zin cing /
'dir sa khong tsam du /
mngon spyod spyi 'gro'i sreg pa hom gyi gzer kha bskal pa'i me chen zhes pa bzhugs so /
!
/bzhi pa rlung la bskur ba'i las ni /
yi dam so so dang 'brel ba'i 'phang ba zor gyi man ngag 'ga' zhig sngar bkod pa rnams yin la /
rlung la las bcol ba'i 'khor lo'i man ngag ni /
sum pa byang chub blo gros kyi dregs pa nyi shu'i rlung 'khor dang /
gshin rje tshe bdag gi rna cha brgyad kyi nang gses rlung nag 'byed pa'i 'khor lo dang don gcig tu bzhed pa a tsar+Ya 'jigs med zhabs la 'bro lo shes rab grags kyis gsan cing snga 'gyur gyi phyogs su bka' babs pa khams gsum 'khrugs byed rlung nag las kyi 'khor lo /
dri med lhun po dang /
rat+na'i klong gsal gyi las mtha' phung byed las kyi rlung dmar sogs rgya cher bzhugs pa ni 'dir bsdu bar ma nus la /
gter ston g.yas ban ya bon gyis pra dun rtse /
ston pa shAkya 'od kyis lha sa /
sbur bu bya mgon gyis bum thang bcas gter gnas gsum nas so sor bzhes shing /
slar rig 'dzin pad+ma gling pas bum thang nas yang gter du bzhes pas gter ston bzhi tshogs kyi gdams pa rlung 'khor srog gi mchan pa nag po ni gong du pad gling man ngag gter phran gyi khong du bkod zin /
'dir de dang 'dra min dum pa rgya ston chen pos pha bong g.yu sgong nas gdan drangs pa'i rlung 'khrugs 'bum gyi yang snying dug gi 'khor lo lag len dpe'u ris dang bcas pa tsam bzhugs so //
'di'i brgyud pa gong gi bsad pa stag byang ma dang 'dra'o //
spyir gshin rje tshe bdag lcags 'dra lcags sdig yang zlog bcas 'bri byang gi rig sngags 'chang ba rnams nas rim par brgyud de da lta'i bar phyag len gyi rgyun ma nyams pa dang /
'jam dpal khro chu dug sdong 'bri lugs dang /
chags med rin po ches chog bsgrigs kyi gzhung /
byad zlog bsad khang bco lnga pa rjes 'brel bcas /
bsad pa srog sgrub tsit+ta dmar 'byin /
rlung 'khor sogs shin tu zab rgyas phyag len can /
king kang bka' ma gshin rje nyi ma bzhi pa'i man ngag dgra bo shwa 'ded /
khro chu bka' ma gshin rje khrag sob tu grags pa sogs kyi rgyun phyag bzhes dang bcas pa dang /
gzhan yang gong du snga phyir 'phros don smos pa de rnams phal cher gyi rgyun bzhugs par snang zhing /
mngon spyod kyi las phran skor yang nyang gter rta nag gi bsad las /
chos dbang rin po che'i phung byed sAts+tsha smyon pa dang /
ngan sngags lto ba sum dkrugs /
gnubs kyi gong khug sro ma can gyi shog dril bcu zhar byung rdzas mthu bcas 'bri gung chos grags kyi bla rdo gshin rje'i be bum nag po'am gnubs kyi gong khug brgya rtsa /
gnubs kyi gdams pa thor bu'i skor las /
mdze nag dang sbal pa'i gson gtad /
gshor brdabs chog
/'byed pa rta g.yag ma /
nye 'byed se shing ma /
dgra bo'i bsod nams sbubs pa /
gnod sbyin rA dza'i nor snyegs /
gnubs chen rnam 'phrul rgya ston brtson 'grus seng ge dar gyi zab gter rdo rje brag btsan /
sangs gling dgongs 'dus btsan rgod dang /
srog thun dug chu khol ma /
rat+na'i drag dmar gyi thems med rkun ma mgo 'khor /
rta gsang gi mi rgod jag chings /
thugs rje gsang 'dus kyi bka' srung ngas nus ma'i cho 'phrul /
gnubs chen rnam 'phrul dri med kun dga'i a tsa ra khrom rgyug
/bdud 'dul zhing skyong /
klong gsal btsan rgod khro 'bar /
rol rdor gyi chos srung skor dang /
yod dge'i trak+shad kyi las mtha' sogs zab gter so so dang 'brel ba'i skor ci rigs pa dang /
phung bon mgo dmar gyi dam can byes chas /
chu gtad nag po zlog med /
thub pa nag po'i mgo 'khor /
a tsa ra dzu nag gi phung byed thal ba'i skor /
mu stegs nag po khrag ral /
drag sngags sha ba rgyug 'gyel /
srog mthu rkyal ba phus 'debs /
btsan thabs la btsas gza' 'gyed /
ngan thabs bya rgod sgro bcings /
ltas ngan spral dmar gla skya /
cho 'phrul mon pa sgo brdung sogs bka' gter gang yin dmigs kyis ma bsal yang rno myur phyag bzhes dang /
rbad khams can mang du bzhugs par grags mod /
'dir de tsam gyis 'thus par byas shing /
sngags 'bum za yig mngon spyod kyi las rgyun ldan 'ga' zhig ni bka' rgya ma'i glegs bam du bzhugs par byas so //
yang gnubs chung gi dbang phyug se yan pa /
'brom ston chung gi re ma tI'i srog mthu yul khams phung byed /
zla ban gzi brjid kyi sngags sdeb /
bla ma phyag rdor ba'i gza'i drag sngags /
o rgyan gling pa'i rA hu la gnad 'bebs /
nyang ring shes rab grags dang /
nyang ston dbang chen bzang po'i gza'i gdong gtad /
a tsa ra dmar po'i phung byed gri thal ma /
rdor gling bram ze sbu gu'i drag sngags /
shes rab me 'bar gyi re ma tI'i cho 'phrul /
kun skyong gling pa'i zhing skyong mi phreng dmar po /
pad+ma dbang rgyal gyi dam can skyer mdung can gyi cho 'phrul /
gro shul las 'phro gling pa'i drag sngags reg phung nag po rnams zab cing /
phyag bzhes can yin tshul dge slong phyag rdor ba'i man ngag gi zin tho sogs su snang mod deng sang rgyun bzhugs min ma 'tshal lo //
mthar thug gi mngon spyod ni /
gong 'og tu smos pa'i rim gnyis zab mo'i rnal 'byor rjong 'phrang srog gsum gyi skya bar nas bton te nyams su blangs pas /
gzung 'dzin bag chags dang bcas pa'i dgra gsum bsad bdud bzhi bcom /
'phrang gsum bsal nas he ru ka'i go 'phang tshe 'dir mngon du byed pa'i thabs ji snyed pa rnams so //
spyir las kyi tshogs la /
rgyud sde chen po rnams nas dman pa zhi sogs las rab 'byams dang /
'bring grub pa brgyad dang /
mchog mkha' spyod dang rig pa 'dzin pa'i go 'phang zhes gsungs pa las /
'dir gtso bor las dang po la nye bar mkho ba'i dbang du byas nas thun mong zhi sogs kyi las tshogs nyid bshad pa yin la de la'ang dgyes rdor las /
dbang dang mngon spyod dang /
dgra'i sde 'jig pa dang /
bskrad pa dang /
bsad pa dang /
dgug pa dang /
zhi ba dang /
rgyas par yang 'gyur ro zhes las chen brgyad gsungs pa'ang rtsa ba'i las bzhir 'du ste dgug pa la dbang dang mngon spyod kyis dgug pa gnyis yod cing /
dgra'i sde 'jig pa sogs lhag ma bzhi mngon spyod kyi bye brag go
/des mtshon te sgyu 'phrul khog gzhung las /
ro langs tshe dang pra sgrub dang //
zhes sogs thun mong dang /
yi ge sgyu 'phrul tshogs sgrub dang //
sogs mchog gi dngos grub sgrub pa'i thabs ji snyed cig gsungs pa rnams kyang gnas skabs dang mthar thug gi las bzhi'i khongs su 'du ba'i tshul rgya cher spros pas chog go
/thun mong gi las tshogs rab 'byams 'di rnams deng dus rang gzhan gyi chen por rloms pa phal cher lto 'grangs nyi mas dros nas rkyen glo bur ma byung ba'i tshe de 'dras ci bya zhes 'phongs phyis pa'i rdo bzhin du dor ste seng ge ltar smin ma gzeng      gtod pas 'gying zhing /
rkyen dang dgos pa cung zad byung ba'i tshe wa skyes las kyang zhum pa zhig byas te bon po'i btsan mchod mkhan /
'dre mthong ba'i klu bcos mkhan /
kla klo'i char 'bebs mkhan tshun chad la skyabs bcol nas mthe bo sgrengs te sdod dgos pa'i ya mtshan la dgod bro ba mang po mthong bas /
de dag gis kyang dgos dus phan bde dal dus 'tshol na ci ma rung snyam mo //
gzhan du jo bo bka' gdams pa'i dge bshes gong ma rnams kyis mchog gtso bor bton /
las tshogs gtso bor mi bton gsungs pa'i rnam thar la mig yar blta'i tshul gyis tshe yun thung /
shes bya rnam grangs mang ba sogs nges 'byung gis rgyud bskul te rkyen gang la'ang ltos pa med par sgrub pa snying por byed pa ni gcig tu ngo mtshar bas rjes su yi rangs shing thal mo lan brgyar sbyar ba'i yul lo //
las sgrub pa'i skabs kyi dbang dang byin rlabs bka' gtad kyi rigs rnams dang gdams skor gtso che ba rnams kyi brgyud pa bkod cing /
gdams phran sil bu sna tshogs pa rnams kyang lung rgyun med pa'i yig sna gang rnyed bsdus pa ni gcig kyang med mod /
phal cher rgyun yod nges pa tsam las brgyud pa'i mtshan mi gsal ba dang /
phyogs mtshon shes pa dag kyang re re nas bkod na ha cang yig tshogs che bar 'gyur zhing /
rgyun yod nges pas 'thus pa las de tsam dgos gal can du'ang ma mngon pas spros pa'i rtsol ba ma byas kyang /
zur tsam mtshon na /
rdor gling sogs gter kha gsum ldan gyi bzlas chog sngags 'bum dkar po /
nyang gter rdzas srung dang shing bu drug pa'i srung ba /
phyugs nad srung gso khams pa me zor gyi gter ma sogs /

dbang gi cho ga
/brgyud pa dbang lung gnyis ka snga ma dang mtshungs /
gter chen de nyid kyi zab gter thugs dam zab pa skor bdun la rgyud lung man ngag gsum re'i tshul du bzhugs pa lcags byang ma'i skor rnams rgyud /
zangs byang ma lung /
mchong byang smug po man ngag gi skor du gtso bor bzhugs par gsungs pa las /
lcags byang ma'i skor phal mo che gtan la phab grub pa las sgyu 'phrul dang dong sprugs tsam ma gtogs pa gzhan rnams sgrub pa sde brgyad skabs su song zin /
'dir ye rgyal nam mkha' mdzod zangs shog dmar po'i chos sde las byon pa lung lugs rta mgrin gyi gtor dbang /
rta mgrin snying po don 'dus kyi sgrub phrin gter gzhung /
dbang chog

//spyi don gsum pa man ngag rdzogs pa chen po a ti yo ga la /

/zhes rnam pa gsum du mchis pa las /
dang po phyi sems sde'i skor la /
bod du thog mar byon cing grags che ba slob dpon chen po bai ro tsa na'i bka' srol rim pa lngar grags pa las brgyud de /
sgyus nyang rma gsum /
'khon zur gnubs gsum /
skor rong khams gsum /
sri'u skyal skye gsum sogs kyi lugs srol mtha' yas pa zhig byung na'ang /
phyis su nyang lugs sam bka' sde zur pa'i srol dang /
khams lugs sam a ro lugs su grags pa gnyis po grags che ba las /
snga ma la sems sde a don bco brgyad kyi rig pa'i rtsal dbang dang zab khrid bcas bzhugs shing /
phyi ma la smin grol gyi skor rgya cher mchis kyang deng sang rgyun dkon par mngon la /
de dag gi rgyab rten /
kun byed rgyal po'i skor /
sems smad bco brgyad kyi skor /
gu ru ye shes khyung grags kyi gter ma gser gyi rus sbal sogs sems sde spyi'i skor rnams te rgyud sde rab 'byams kyi lung dang /
bskyed pa'i rim pa sgrub sde brgyad dang /
rdzogs rim sems phyogs kyi man ngag mthar thug gtso bor bton pa'i bka' brgyad rdzong 'phrang gi smin grol rnams kyi rgyun ma nub par bzhugs la /
gter ma'i phyogs su    pod gnyis tsam   de mtshungs rgyud dang smin grol rkang tshugs bzhugs par ma mthong yang /
gu ru rin po che'i zhal lung phyag chen gyi gdams pa rnams sems phyogs dang 'brel bar mngon /
de la'ang zhar las byon pa ni shin tu mang yang dmigs su bsal ba nyang gter bla ma dmar khrid las phyag chen sangs rgyas lag 'chang rim pa gnyis /
sangs gling bla ma dgongs 'dus kyi klong yangs mtha' bral /
don tig dang zab tig gnyis kyi gnyug ma gcer mthong /
bstan gnyis gling pa'i 'khor ba rtsad gcod /
bdud 'dul rdo rje'i phyag chen rig gnyis sogs mang du byon par snang yang phal cher rgyun ma bzhugs pa dang /
'ga' zhig chos sde'i rgyun phyogs gcig tu bzhugs pas khol 'don ma dgos la /
'dir sprul pa'i gter chen pad+ma 'od gsal mdo sngags gling pa'i yang gter o rgyan dri med kun dga'i phyag rgya chen po'i khrid /
khrid yig gter gzhung /
brgyud pa gong gsal thugs rje chen po rgyal ba rgya mtsho ltar la /
gter chen bla ma dngos las bka' drin du thob pa'o //

/gnyis pa klong sde la /
rgyud klong chen rab 'byams rgyal po'i rgyud sogs    pod gcig tsam gyi    ni rgyud 'bum du bzhugs la /
smin grol man ngag bcas rang rkang tshugs pa ni snyan brgyud rdo rje zam pa tsam du mngon la /
lam srol zab mo 'di la brten nas lo chen bai ro tsa na nas brtsams te brgyud pa bdun gyi bar du ye shes 'od skur gshegs pa sha stag byon cing /
de nas kyang grub mchog brnyes pa bar ma chad du byon nas da lta'i dus kyang nyams pa med par bzhugs pa la dbang gdams rgyab rten dang bcas pa'i gzhung rgya cher mchis /
gzhan yang klong sde'i skor gyi gdams ngag gi gnad phal cher kha rag skor gsum dang /
lce sgom pa'i man ngag sogs las 'byung ba sngar dar rgyas che bar byung snang yang deng sang rgyun med par mngon /
grub pa'i dbang phyug thang stong rgyal po la ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro rdo rje phag mos dngos su gnang ba'i snyan brgyud gsang spyod rin po che'i skor las /
dbang bzhi pa'i lam thams cad klong sde'i man ngag ji lta bar gsungs te smin grol gyi rgyun yang legs par bzhugs snang /
de tsam las gter ma'i phyogs su klong sde'i gdams skor rkang tshugs byon par ma thos la /
gter gsar rdzogs chen sde gsum gras su smin grol kha tshang bzhugs yod par snang yang rang nas thos pa'i skal pa ma byung bas phyin chad 'byon pa rnams kyis 'dir sa bcad mi stong ba'i phyir bzhugs par zhu'o /

/gsum pa gsang ba man ngag gi sde la /
spyir grub chen dam pa sangs rgyas la slob dpon rin po ches dngos su gnang ba'i rdzogs chen gyi skor dang /
rje btsun mi las kyang rdzogs chen gyi gdams skor gter nas bzhes par grags shing /
zhang g.yu brag pa'i thugs bcud rdzogs pa chen po dang /

gtso bor sems sde dang man ngag sde'i phyi nang gi skor du gtogs par nges /
gang ltar yang phyi nang thun mong dang /
gsang skor dang /

gsang skor bka' ma gtso bor bton pa snyan brgyud thig le gsang skor du grags pa'i smin grol gyi rgyun yang mchis so //

/gnyis pa slob dpon chen po pad+ma'i bka' srol ni /

/'jigs med gling pa'i klong chen snying tig sogs zab gter phal mo che'i rdzogs chen gyi skor rnams dang /
'brug pa rgyal dbang rje la slob dpon rin po ches dngos su gnang ba'i rdzogs chen pad+ma snying tig tu grags pa sogs ji snyed cig byon kyang /

/brgyud pa tshe sgrub 'od zer drwa ba dang 'dra'o //
gter chen de nyid kyis sbrags yang rdzong nas spyan drangs pa rdzogs chen hU~M skor snying thig gi bla ma'i bum dbang /
yi dam gsang dbang /
mkha' 'gro'i sher dbang /
tshig dbang /
gdams gtad dbang rnams dang /

/gsum pa slob dpon chen po bai ro tsa na'i bka' srol ni /
rdo rje gling pas gnam lcags brag nas spyan drangs pa'i snying tig bcu gsum gyi nang tshan bai ro'i snying tig dum bu sum cu pa dang /
kun skyong gling pa'i rdzogs chen bai ro'i gong khug mar grags pa sogs dmigs kyis bsal ba ci rigs byung mod kyang /
deng sang rgyun bzhugs par ma mngon la /
'on kyang slob dpon rnam gnyis kyi bka' srol du don gyis tshang /
'dir sa bcad tsam du gu ru rin po ches lo chen bai ro tsa na la ched du bstsal cing /
de nyid kyis kyang lha bu don yod sde la sogs pa la sger du gdams shing gter gnas rnams su rgyas btab pa gter ston rnams kyis rim par bton pa'i zab chos rdor sems snying thig tu grags pa'i chos skor dang po /
gter ston grub thob yongs kyi rgyal po o rgyan rdo rje gling pas chos 'byung zangs kyi mtsho brag nas bzhes /
gnyis pa pad+ma kun skyong gling pas mi tshor rdo rje'i ske brag nas bton /
gsum pa stag sham bsam gtan gling pas bar khams phra mo brag nas spyan drangs pa gsum po thems med kyi chos bka' mang nyung tsam las /
thems can rtsa ba'i chos sde rnams zhu dag pher cing snga ma'i tshig brgyud kyang phyi mas gsan pas chu bo gcig 'dres su gyur pa ma zad /
pad+ma bde chen gling pa la gter ston snga ma gnyis kyi ye shes kyi sku dang /
phyi ma sku dngos kyis gdams pa bstsal pas gter chos gcig gis gsum ka'i rgyun go chod pa las /
'dir dpe rgyun rtsa ba kun skyong gling pa'i gter byon gyi rtsa ba'i dbang bzhi /
stag sham lugs kyi thod rgal dbang /
gsol 'debs gsung rgyun ma /
gter gzhung thems can la /

snying thig gi lo rgyus /

khregs chod /

/bzhi pa slob dpon rnam gsum gyi dgongs nyams gcig tu dril ba ni /
gtso bor byang gter kun bzang dgongs pa zang thal nyid yin la /
dbang khrid rgyab rten bcas ma nub par bzhugs kyang chos bka' rgya che ba'i phyir bsdu bar ma 'tshal bas /
'dir dgongs pa zang thal gyi gnad thams cad bsdus pa'i don khrid bu 'bor ba bkra shis rgya mtshos mdzad pa tsam bzhugs /

bshags skong /

/gnyis pa man ngag sde'i rgyud don zab mo spyi'i gnad ston pa spyi ti yo gar grags pa'i skor la /
snang srid kha sbyor rgyud sogs bka' ma dang nyang gter zung du 'brel ba'i rgyud sde bcu drug tsam gyi rgyun rgyud 'bum rin po cher bzhugs na'ang /
de rnams dang 'brel ba'i smin grol gyi gdams pa ji ltar byung ma 'tshal la /
'dir bstan gnyis gling pa'i thugs sras snang bzhi mthar phyin spa gro ba tshe ring rdo rjes brag dmar gter khung nas spyan drangs pa'i zab mo spyi ti'i dbang bzhi /
kha byang lung bstan /
them byang /
khrid kyi sngon 'gro
/dbang bzhi yongs rdzogs /
dngos gzhi'i zab khrid /
mun khrid ar gtad /
lung bstan /
ka dag lhun grub kyi nyams len /
gter bdag rdor legs gsol mchod bcas gter gzhung tshang ba /
dbang gi lag len bcas bzhugs /
brgyud pa ni /
kun bzang yab yum /
rgyal ba rigs lnga /
o rgyan chen po /
mtsho rgyal /
nus 'byin sa le /
khol mo lha lcam gang 'bum /
gter ston tshe ring rdo rje /
thugs sras kun grol rdo rje /
chos dbang grags pa /
spa gro chos dbang lhun grub /
'bras ljongs pa yon tan dpal bzang /
gtsang pa rdzogs chen pad+ma mi bskyod /
bya btang nyi zla 'od gsal /
zar sprul gsang sngags bstan 'dzin /
kun bzang thugs kyi rdo rje /
dge slong rdo rje bsam gtan /
'di yan gcig brgyud lta bur bzhugs shing snang bzhi mthar phyin pa sha stag byung /

/gsum pa yang gsang thun mong ma yin pa'i snyan brgyud ston pas yang ti yo gar grags pa'i skor la /

hrIHdmar gshin rje'i yang snying /
gter kha bzhi 'dus kyi yang zlog rdo rje pha lam /
bka' gter gnyis ldan king dmar bcas /
gzhan yang las rab 'byams phal mo che lag len byin nus dang ldan pa'i rgyun kho nar snang yang 'dir gtso che ba tsam smos pa yin la /
rdzogs rim gong gi yi dam so so dang 'brel ba'i rigs rnams dang /
dza bIr rigs gsum cong zhi'i bcud len bcas pa /
khros nag srog sgrub sogs kyi gtum mo dang gcod yul /
ma gcig lugs kyi gcod khrid /
rig 'dzin tshe dbang nor bu'i tshe khrid dang thugs rje chen po'i smar khrid /
rdzogs chen mkha' 'gro'i snying tig
/rat+na'i klong gsal snying tig
/a ti zab don snying po /
klong chen snying tig
/yang ti sangs rgyas mnyam sbyor dang gser gyi 'bru gcig rnams nges par nyams su blang dgos pa'i gal po che rnams yin no //
de dag kun gyi snying por gyur pa smin lugs rdor sems /
kar gling zhi khro /
chos dbang bla ma gsang 'dus dang 'ja' tshon spyi 'dus /
thugs rje chen po rgyal po lugs dang rgyal ba rgya mtsho /
rdzogs chen mkha' 'gro snying tig dang sangs rgyas mnyam sbyor te bla rdzogs thugs gsum /
bka' dgongs phur pa /
nyang lugs khros nag rnams shin tu khyad par 'phags pas nyams len snying por bya bar rigs shing /
chos skyong gter kha bzhi 'dus kyi ma ning /
ma gza' dam gsum kun mkhyen lugs kyi gsol mchod kyang 'dor bar mi bya'o //
gter gsar rnams dus skabs dang 'tshams par rgyal ba'i thugs rje las shar ba dang brgyud thag nye zhing dam sel gyis bar du ma chod par byin nus che bas mchog tu bya dgos pa gzhir bcas /
lhag par rtsod bral sprul pa'i gter chen rnam pa gnyis kyi zab chos mtha' dag bka' gter khungs ma dang 'brel zhing lung rigs nyams myong gi tshad mas grub pa ma zad /
kha tshang don 'dril lag len khyer bde ba'i phyir nyams su blang 'os pa sha stag snang bas kha shas tsam las dmigs su smos ma dgos shing /
khyad par du'ang 'chi med rig 'dzin chen po rnam pa gnyis dang zhal mi gnyis pa khyab bdag bla ma pad+ma 'od gsal mdo sngags gling pa'i zab gter las /
bla ma mtsho skyes snying tig
/thugs rje chen po sems nyid ngal gso   mi bzhugs /
rdzogs chen lce btsun snying tig gsum /
snyan brgyud gshin rje yang dag phur pa /
dgongs gter 'phags ma'i snying tig rnams gcig chog tu bzung ba dang /
rtsa gsum dril sgrub /
yig drug gsol 'debs sgrub thabs /
gnyen po lha lnga sogs yang gter gyi rigs rnams dang /
thams cad las kyang bka' 'dus chos kyi rgya mtsho /
spyan ras gzigs rgyal ba rgya mtsho /
rdo rje bdud rtsi /
mkha' 'gro gsang ba kun 'dus rnams snying gi thig le ltar gces par 'dzin pas gser dang ra gan mi snyom par bskyed rdzogs kyi nyams len ji tsam nus par 'bad de zab chos mjal ba don dang ldan par bya'o //
las kyi tshogs ni /
phan byed kyi skor rnams rang nyid nus ldan du bya dgos pas bsnyen sgrub spyi dang bye brag legs par thems nas skabs dang 'brel bar gzhan phan sems bskyed bzang pos brtsam par bya ba dang /
nor sgrub dang dbang sdud sogs rang 'dod kyi 'khris med par bstan 'gro spyi la phan pa'i don kho nar bsgrub par rigs la /
mngon spyod bsad mnan sogs ni rtogs pas bdag rgyud grol nas snying rjes gzhan rgyud 'dren nus pa dang /
bstan pa dang sems can la phan pa rlabs su che nges pa'i gnas mthong na ma gtogs nam du'ang brtsam par bya ba ma yin pa rgyal bas rgyud sde rab 'byams las shin tu bkag pa'i don dran par bya dgos so /
!
/da ni spyir 'phros pa'i don 'di'ang brjod par bya ste /
snga 'gyur rdo rje theg pa'i shing rta chen po rnams la lam srol ni /
dbang /
bshad pa /
bskyed rim /
rdzogs rim ste bka' babs kyi chu bo bzhi zhes yongs su grags pas /
rnying ma ming tsam ma yin par lugs mthun zhig byed na /
sngar dngos dang 'phros don gyi skabs su ji skad smos pa'i bka' ma'i gzhung bzang po mtha' dag gam /
mdo sgyu sems gsum gyi rtsa ba re re'i smin grol gyi sgo phye ste /
sgyu 'phrul gsang ba snying po'i rgyud kyi bshad srol la sgro 'dogs legs par bcad /
gter ma'i phyogs nas bka' dgongs phur gsum dang /
gshin rje tshe bdag
/rta mgrin yang gsang /
phyag rdor dregs pa kun 'dul gyis mtshon bka' brgyad bye brag pa'i skor rnams dang /
bla sgrub dang thugs rje chen po'i skor ci rigs /
rdzogs chen snying tig ya bzhi dang zab mo yang tig
/kun mkhyen klong chen pa'i dgongs gter gyi bstan bcos mdzod bdun /
ngal gso skor gsum cha lag dang bcas pa rnams kyi steng 'di nyid nas 'byung ba'i smin grol las tshogs bcas mtha' dag dang /
de dag gi rgyab rten du rgyud 'bum rin po che yongs su rdzogs pa bcas la thos bsam gyi gzhir bzung nas /
bka' mas gzhung bsrang /
gter ma'i man ngag gis nyams su blangs te /
yi dam gyi mngon rtogs chung ngu zhig nyams su len kyang /
rgyu shes pa'i mtshan nyid de bzhin nyid kyi lta bas thag bcad tshul /
rkyen 'jug pa'i mtshan nyid ting nge 'dzin gyis nyams su blang tshul /
de las lam gyur gyi 'bras bu rig 'dzin rnam bzhi'i grub mthar ji ltar snyog pa'i tshul la nges pa gting tshugs pas gzhung gdams ngag tu 'char zhing /
gdams ngag gzhung dang mi 'gal ba zhig gal che bas /
'brel med kyi tha snyad nyi tshe dang rtog ge'i tshig skam re gnyis smra ba la bshad pa dang /
yi dam gyi rgyun khyer re dang /
chos skyong gi gtor skong re chags med byed pa la sgrub pa dang /
gtor zlog gi 'ur shog re la las sbyor du ming btags nas rang gzhung yin nges dang dgos nges rnams dor ba'i rjes su 'brang bar mi bya'o //
bye brag tu /
gzhung 'di nyid kyi smin grol legs par thob nas gzhan la 'bogs par 'dod pas rab gong du bshad pa'i gal po che'i yi dam mtha' dag gam /
'bring de las snying por gyur pa rnams dang /
ma mtha' yang rigs thams cad kyi khyab byed rdo rje sems dpa'/
byin rlabs thams cad kyi 'jug sgo bla sgrub gang rung /
dkyil 'khor thams cad kyi dbye gzhi sgrub pa bka' brgyad rnams kyi bsnyen pa las rung dang /
rdzogs chen gang rigs kyi nyams khrid smin par thob cing nyams myong gi sne cung zad zin pa zhig gis bya ba las /
dpe klog dag po'ang mi shes bzhin du chos la dbang za bas rdo rje slob dpon gyi go sar 'gying bar mi bya la /
slob ma rnams kyis kyang spyir dam tshig dang sdom pa dag par bya bas gzhi bzung ste /
yi dam rtsa ba gang rung re'i bsnyen sgrub kyi dam bca' dang /
chos srung rnams la rgyun nam dus kyi mchod gtor ma chag tsam re bya bas mtshon /
mdor na bstan pa dang rang rgyud la dmigs pa'i lhag bsam rnam par dag pas go phye ste 'chad nyan la 'jug par mdzad na /
bshad pa dang /
sgrub pa dang /
rgyal ba dgyes pa'i phrin las la brten nas srid pa dang zhi ba'i legs tshogs kyi sgo thams cad rgya cher 'phel zhing rgyas par 'gyur ro //
bdag 'dra blo gros dman kyang chos rgyus che //
yon tan chung yang dam pas rjes su bzung //
phyogs gcig sdod kyang dag snang phyogs ris med //
mkhos chung lhag bsam che ba'i lag rjes so //
bstan la bsams nas zas chos 'bad pas btsal //
ma mthong g.yang sar ma mchongs bag yod byas //
grags rjes ma rgyugs tshad ma'i rjes su 'brangs //
deng dus kha cig rgan rabs 'dod gtam dang //
gter lung phyogs re tsam la yid brton nas //
lung dang rigs pa dpang bzhag lta ci smos //
gzu bo'i blo yis brtag dpyad cang med par //
'ga' zhig lha dang phal cher bdud kyis 'phrul //
'di ni chos yin 'di ni chos min zhes //
dam pa dmod cing chos spang las ngan gsog
/snyigs dus bdud dang dam sri'i cho 'phrul dang //
lta log chos min 'byung ba bden mod kyang //
zag med mngon shes chos spyan ldan ma gtogs //
de dag ji bzhin shes pa shin tu dka'//
ngag rgyun 'ga' yang legs par khungs dpyad na //
nges par mkhas shing grub pa'i phrin las kyi //
gzi brjid phyogs su lhung rnams bzod min pas //
'gran las rgyal phyir rang phyogs ci thod du //
'bros khungs btsal ba'i cal rjes rgyugs pa las //
gtan tshigs gzhan med khrel ba'i gnas kyang mthong //
gter ston tshad ma'i lung bstan yin gyur kyang //
mtha' gcig nges pa'i don du bzung byar min //
dgongs gzhi dgos pa dngos la gnod byed mang /
khyad par 'phral rkyen rten 'brel gzhan dbang btsan //
thog tu ma khel bzang ngan go ldog dang //
snga phyir 'gal ba ltag sprod bris pa'ang mthong //
drang don lung dang zag bcas mngon shes kyis //
lkog gyur gnas la spar tshod bya mi dgos //
bla ma bzang ngan brgyud 'dzin slob mas shes //
bzang la mang na dam pa yin pa'i rtags //
yon tan med na slob ma bzang mi 'byung //
blun pos bkur ba tsam la snying po med //
gter ston ci 'dra chos brgyud 'phel 'bris shes //
chos 'phel 'gro don che na tshad ma'i rtags //
gter rdzun 'das nas chos rgyun nub par gsungs //
ltar snang mthu nus la sogs 'byung po'i 'phrul //
des na brton pa bzhi la yid brton nas //
blang dor shes na skyes bu dam pa'i tshul //
ma shes phyogs lhung bral ba'i gzu bo'i blos //
gzhan gyi yon tan brtags nas dang du len //
bskyed rdzogs zab rgyas rnams la smos ci dgos //
gdams ngag phran tshegs res kyang gna' dus nas //
deng bar 'gro phan mdzad 'di gu ru rje'i //
byin rlabs thugs rje'i stobs su nges pa rnyed //
de phyir da dung 'jig rten phan bde'i btsas //
yun ring 'tsho gzhes bzhugs phyir ngal ba brgyas //
bka' bsdu byas 'di rtag cing khyab pa yi //
bkra shis rtsa gsum srung mas stsol bar mdzod //
mngon shes mi ldan 'khrul pa'i dbang gyur pas //
mos blos brtsams kyang nongs pa'i rnyogs pa kun //
skyabs mchog thugs rje'i nor bus bgrungs nas kyang //
dag byed tshad ma skye dgu'i yun 'tshor shog
/'di las dkar po rnam par 'phel ba'i cha //
yar zla bzhin du 'phel zhing rab rgyas pas //
rtog sgrib mun pa kun bsal rnam grol gyi //
snang ba dam pas sa gsum khyab gyur cig
/ces dus zhabs snyigs ma'i skye dgu mchog dman yongs la 'phral dang yun du gang la gang 'tshams kyi phan bde nor bu'i gru char mdzad med du 'jo ba la mtshungs pa'i zla dang bral ba'i gsung rab rin po che /
sangs rgyas gnyis pa pad+mA ka ra'i thugs bskyed dang phrin las las snang bar gyur pa'i zab mo gter gyi chos tshad mar gyur pa gtso che ba rnams phyogs su bsdus pa rin chen gter gyi mdzod chen por ji ltar bzhugs pa'i tshogs dang gang las brgyud pa rags rim bcas pa'i dkar chag 'di'ang /
rgyal dbang pad+ma'i sngags rig 'dzin pa pad+ma gar gyi dbang phyug phrin las 'gro 'dul rtsal lam rgyal ba'i sras po blo gros mtha' yas kyis zab lung gnyis pa rdzong shod bde gshegs 'dus pa'i sgrub gnas chen por grub par bgyis pa dge legs 'phel //
